East Chahar Situation Tense, Outposts Still Distant 6

Puppet troops gathered and awaiting orders.

The authorities ordered the front lines to maintain calm.

Matsui and Yue Kai-xian engaged in preliminary negotiations.

Yue Kai-xian's Telegram Stated That the Situation Is Not Expected to Escalate 7

(Tianjin) A portion of the puppet Rehe army, Zhang Junzhe's brigade and Peng Jinsheng's brigade, approximately over three thousand cavalry and infantry, arrived at Datang, Fengning County, on the Chahar border. This army was transferred from the Weichang and Luanping counties and is under the command of Japanese training officers and brigade adjutants. They are awaiting orders in the area. Over a thousand troops from Li Shouxin's puppet Rehe Garrison Brigade have gathered within the territory of the third and fourth districts of Guyuan, with the majority being transported forward from Duolun. The situation in East Chahar is tense. However, the outposts of both sides are still forty li apart and have not made contact. Lieutenant Colonel Matsui, the Japanese Kwantung Army military attache stationed in Zhangjiakou, flew back to Zhangyuan from Changchun on the 19th, carrying orders from his superiors to convey to the Chahar authorities. Although Chahar Province Chairman Song Zheyuan is in Beiping, he has telegraphed orders to all his troops to remain calm and firmly defend their positions. (20th Dispatch)

(Beiping) Yue Kai-xian met with Matsui, the Japanese military attache stationed in Zhangjiakou, to discuss the East Chahar matter. He telegraphed Beiping today, reporting that he had met with Matsui and that the East Chahar incident is not expected to escalate. (20th Dispatch)

(Beiping) After the East Chahar issue arose, the diplomatic envoys of various countries stationed in Beiping have paid close attention. Foreign newspaper reporters stationed in Beiping have all received telegrams instructing them to immediately rush to the area to investigate the truth. (20th Dispatch)

(Beiping) Beiping received a report from East Chahar this morning stating that besides a small number of puppet troops stationed in the Datang area, which is twenty li from Guyuan, there are only four Japanese individuals staying there. The rumor that there are three thousand Japanese and puppet troops is not factual. Over two thousand cavalry from Zhang Haipeng's puppet army are currently stationed in Chengde. In the areas of Changliang, Wunihu, South Shizhuzi, North Shizhuzi, and Shidaogou in East Chahar, the total number of our local militia is no more than two hundred. Regular troops of the 29th Army have not been stationed in the area. Although Japanese and puppet troops have occasionally scattered leaflets and slogans in the area in recent days, claiming that they will begin military action, there has been no contact. Our authorities have only ordered the front lines to maintain strict defense and not to act rashly, maintaining a very calm attitude. At the same time, both Chinese and Japanese authorities believe that it is a local incident and not a major problem. It is currently being negotiated by Matsui, the Japanese military attache stationed in Zhangyuan, and Yue Kaixian, the special diplomatic envoy of Chahar Province. Song Zheyuan's return to Chahar has not yet been determined. Yue Kai-xian came to Beiping from Zhangyuan yesterday afternoon to report to Song Zheyuan on the recent situation in East Chahar and to attend last night's banquet held by Song Zheyuan for the Japanese military attache Takahashi Tan. He stayed overnight in Beiping and will return to Zhangyuan this afternoon. (20th Dispatch)

(Beiping) A certain provincial committee stated that it was unexpected and regrettable that the Japanese side intended to begin military action on the grounds that Changliang and Wunihu were within the borders of Fengning County. Although the Japanese side has made various statements, the current situation in East Chahar is still peaceful and there are no abnormalities. Although the Japanese side has made various statements about what they will do, they have not yet officially submitted a protest to our authorities through diplomatic channels. According to Takahashi Tan, the military attache of the Japanese embassy, the East Chahar issue is a local incident and is being negotiated by Matsui with the Chahar authorities, and a resolution should not be difficult. (20th Dispatch)

(Beiping) The Japanese army has a regiment stationed in Rehe Province, as well as four airplanes and four tanks. The leaflets scattered in Chahar Province previously were dropped from these airplanes. (20th Dispatch)

(Tianjin) Someone visited Takahashi Tan, the military attache of the Japanese embassy in Beiping this morning. According to him, his meetings with Song Zheyuan in recent days were for other matters unrelated to this incident. This matter falls under the responsibility of the military authorities, and he is not responsible for making contact. (20th Dispatch)

(Nanjing) The Japanese and puppet troops in Rehe Province, using the excuse that Changliang and Wunihu belong to Fengning County in Rehe Province, have launched a military action. After receiving the report, Song Zheyuan has sent two telegrams to Nanjing reporting on the situation. (20th Dispatch)

(Beiping) The East Chahar issue can be resolved peacefully. Takahashi, the military attache of the Japanese embassy, stated on the 20th that this is a local issue and that the Japanese side has appointed Matsui, the Japanese military attache stationed in Zhangyuan, to be responsible for the negotiations, and it will be resolved soon. Our side also believes that it is a local incident and has ordered Yue Kaixian, the special diplomatic envoy of Chahar, to make contact nearby. Yue Kai-xian came to Beiping from Zhangyuan on the 18th to report everything to Song Zheyuan and will return to Chahar on the 20th. After arriving in Zhangyuan, he will begin negotiations with Matsui. Changliang, Wunihu, North Shizhuzi, South Shizhuzi, and Sidaogou are currently maintained by the local militia. The 29th Army has not stationed troops in the area. (20th Central Dispatch)

(Beiping) Due to the transfer of military and police forces on the border between Chahar and Rehe in recent days, misunderstandings between the two sides were unavoidable, and the situation was once quite tense. However, due to the efforts of both sides to avoid conflict and explain the misunderstandings, the situation has gradually eased and is definitely not as serious as rumored. (20th Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Beiping) Xiao Zhenying stated that there are approximately 20,000 Japanese and puppet troops stationed in Rehe Province, including 2,000 Japanese troops. It is rumored that there are only four or five Japanese troops in Datang on the Rehe border, besides a small number of puppet troops. The area is currently maintained by the local militia, and the situation is still very peaceful. Chairman Song Zheyuan's return to Chahar has not yet been scheduled. Song Zheyuan's banquet for the Japanese military attache Takahashi at his private residence on the evening of the 19th was merely a social gathering, and the East Chahar issue was not discussed during the meal. ((20th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Rumor that Zuo Yitong Arrived in Beiping to Meet with He Yingqin to Report on Military and Political Affairs 8

(Beiping) It is rumored that Zuo Yitong and Zhao Chengzhou arrived in Beiping tonight to meet with He Yingqin to report on the situation of suppressing the Yang Monkey bandits. (20th Dispatch)

(Beiping) Zuo Yitong left Taiyuan eastward last night and is expected to arrive in Beiping tonight. Those who came with him include Zhao Daiwen and others. In addition to meeting with He Yingqin to report on the recent situation of military and political affairs in Suiyuan Province, Zuo Yitong will also contact Shen Chang to discuss the railway tracks near Qixiaying that were previously destroyed by floods, and it is planned to use military engineering to rebuild and reroute them. (20th Dispatch)

(Taiyuan) Commander-in-Chief Chiang Kai-shek, in order to eliminate the source of trouble in the border areas as soon as possible due to the scattering of small bands of Yang Monkey bandits, has telegraphed the authorities in Shanxi, Suiyuan, Chahar, and Shaanxi to discuss joint defense and thoroughly eliminate them. Zhao Chengzhou has dispatched an additional regiment of cavalry to Dongsheng to assist in the battle. Yang Hucheng and Shao Lizi, representing Li Zhigang, returned to Shaanxi today to report back. (20th Dispatch)

(Beiping) He Yingqin visited the Summer Palace with his family today. (20th Dispatch)

Yutian Militia Conflict Disrupted Local Order 9

(Beiping) A person from Yutian reported that conflicts between the Yutian militia and police have occurred repeatedly. Recently, bandits have taken advantage of the opportunity to rise up, devastating the local area. The local order has become increasingly chaotic, and the people are unable to make a living. Many have fled to Zunhua, Jixian, Fengrun, Beiping, Tianjin, and other places. (20th Dispatch)

(Tianjin) The Yutian security team has been openly kidnapping villagers every night, extorting money and weapons. If they do not pay, they are labeled as communists, detained, and not released, or executed directly, resulting in many innocent deaths. On the 18th, Li Weisun, a wealthy gentleman from Zhushuwu Town in the fifth district, was invited to talk by two security team leaders under the pretense of discussing matters, and the district police chief was also lured to the suburbs. After being extorted 300 yuan in cash and a gun, they were released. This happened several times a day, and those who had the means to flee all escaped. (20th Dispatch)

(Beiping) Yin Rugeng went to Tianjin today to meet with Yu Xuezhong to discuss how to deal with the conflict between the Yutian militia. He will return to Beiping in the next few days. (20th Dispatch)

Suspects Arrested in Huaitong Bureau Bombing Case 10

(Tianjin) After the bombing at the Shanhaiguan Huaitong Transfer Bureau, the Special Public Security Bureau sent out detectives and arrested eleven suspects. After detailed interrogation, three of them were considered the most suspicious and will be sent to Tianjin within days to be handed over to the provincial government for legal proceedings. Huang Zigang, the manager of the Huaitong Transfer Bureau, stated that the Huaitong Transfer Bureau undertakes transfer matters inside and outside the Guan, and it is purely a commercial operation with no political implications. The bombing was likely due to some people not understanding the organization and position of the bureau. It is regrettable, but his colleagues are determined to continue serving the country with an indomitable spirit. (20th Dispatch)

No Definite Date for New Interior Minister Huang Fu to Assume Office 11

(Nanjing) After arriving in Nanjing, the new Interior Minister Huang Fu has been busy with social engagements. This morning, Gan Naikwang, the Vice Minister of the Interior, visited Huang at his residence to inquire about the date of his assumption of office. Huang stated that he still needed to make some arrangements and had not made a definite decision. Subsequently, Huang met with Commander-in-Chief Chiang Kai-shek and President Wang Jingwei, responded to visits from old friends in Nanjing, and met with Xu Xiuzhi and others who came from Beiping. (20th Dispatch)

Wang Chonghui Met with Chiang Kai-shek and Wang Jingwei 12

Discussed Cooperation with Hu Hanmin in Detail

(Nanjing) Wang Chonghui came to Nanjing last week to wait for an audience with Commander-in-Chief Chiang Kai-shek and has met with him twice. He met with Chiang again on the morning of the 20th and talked for a long time. Wang visited President Wang Jingwei in the afternoon and met with various Central Committee members in Nanjing. They had detailed discussions on cooperation with Hu Hanmin. It is expected that he will go to Shanghai in the next few days, and it has not yet been completely decided whether he will re-enter Nanjing or go abroad to resume his post directly. Yan Huiqing, the ambassador to the Soviet Union, is scheduled to come to Nanjing from Tianjin in the middle of next month. After taking leave, he will take the road through Xinjiang to Russia. Zhang Yuanfu, the former representative of Xinjiang stationed in Nanjing, will accompany Yan to Xinjiang at that time. (20th Dispatch)

Chiang Kai-shek Visited the Mausoleum Yesterday 13

(Nanjing) After arriving in Nanjing, Commander-in-Chief Chiang Kai-shek met with various important figures and handled important matters, which kept him very busy. On the morning of the 20th, as it was Sunday, he went to the mausoleum to visit. In the afternoon, he took a short rest at the official residence of the military academy. An expanded memorial week will be held at the military academy on the morning of the 21st, and military and police officials will participate, with Chiang Kai-shek presiding and delivering a report. (20th Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Nanjing) Commander-in-Chief Chiang Kai-shek is scheduled to attend and give a speech at the expanded memorial week at the military academy on the 21st. All military and police personnel above the rank of major in Nanjing will attend to listen to the speech. Due to insufficient space in the auditorium, it will be held on the parade ground. (20th Dispatch)

Earthquake Occurred in Tangshan 14

(Tianjin) At 3:20 AM on the 19th, an earthquake suddenly occurred in Tangshan. It was very slight at first, then became severe. Tables, chairs, beds, and tents were overturned, and the shaking moved from east to west, lasting about three minutes. Several dilapidated workshops in the eastern mining area of the city collapsed. (20th Dispatch)

Liu's Bandits Looted Along the Way 15

(Tianjin) At 9 PM on the 18th, Liu Guitang's bandit troops moved into the border area between Baodi and Jiahe. At 9 PM, Liu Guitang's bandit troops stood firm and then fled to Dabaizhuang on the border between Baodi and Wuqing. More than 30 villages along the way were looted. They also looted all the major shops and households in Hebeitun, which belongs to Xianghe. The bandit troops forced the villagers to join them, expanding to more than 200 people. Horses and firearms were all searched for and seized from the villages. The militia of Jiahe, Baodi, and Wuqing counties, along with the special police of Jinghai, have rushed to intercept and block them. The province has ordered the security teams of nearby counties to cooperate in the suppression in order to prevent the bandits from fleeing south. (20th Dispatch)

Ministry of Foreign Affairs and Beijing Municipal Government Surveying Embassy Sites 16

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Municipal Government are currently surveying the sites for embassies of various countries in China. There are reports that the Russian and Italian embassies will seek sites for construction first. The government still hopes that the embassies of various countries will gradually move south. (20th Dispatch)

Ministry of Finance Agrees in Principle to Reduce Transaction Tax 17

(Nanjing) It is reported by the Ministry of Finance that the Legislative Yuan is scheduled to hold a review meeting on the transaction tax on the 24th. Telegrams from the councils of various exchanges in Shanghai requesting exemption from or reduction of the tax rate have been arriving at the ministry one after another. The responsible officials have compiled the requests and submitted them to the minister for approval. It is now known that a reduction has been granted in principle, but a complete exemption is not practically possible. (20th Dispatch)

Ministry of Industry Plans Relief for Declining Commerce in the Interior 18

(Nanjing) In recent times, disasters have been frequent, and Chinese rural areas have become bankrupt. Various merchants in Shanghai feel they cannot support the year-end settlements and have sent telegrams calling for relief. Due to the impact of rural areas, commerce in the interior is almost entirely bankrupt. The Ministry of Industry has begun research, with Liang Shangdong, the director of the Commercial Department, drafting a plan in hopes of finding relief measures based on the results of the investigation. It should be completed soon. (20th Dispatch)

Ministry of Finance Plans to Consolidate Local Finances 19

(Nanjing) It is reported that the abolition of exorbitant taxes and miscellaneous fees, with a portion of the business tax and stamp tax used to offset local finances, is limited, and many feel it is insufficient. The finance departments of various provinces have successively requested additional subsidies. Minister of Finance Kong is currently considering this comprehensively. If the provinces issue too many public bonds, they cannot be sold and can only be mortgaged, resulting in great losses, and the burden on the people will increase significantly. In the long run, this is not a normal financial practice. Now that the central and local governments are defining their responsibilities, there should be a method of adjustment under certain normal financial practices. It is said that the demarcation will focus on the suitability of income and expenditure budgets. The provincial governments will be self-sufficient under a certain number. In the past, the finances of Jiangxi and Henan were instructed by the central government. Following this precedent, a detailed opinion will be presented to the Central Political Council to decide on principles first, and then the Ministry of Finance will consult with the authorities of various provinces at length so that this year's local finances can gradually get on the right track. (20th Dispatch)

Internal Organization of the Salt Administration Reform Committee Agreed Upon 20

(Nanjing) The list of candidates for the Salt Administration Reform Committee has been internally finalized. President Wang and Minister of Finance Kong have also decided on the internal organization. Minister Kong will return to Nanjing on Tuesday of this week to attend the Executive Yuan meeting to present it for discussion. Once the candidates are announced, a date will be set to establish the committee and gradually implement the new salt law. (20th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Rumor of the Recovery of Songkan 21

(Chongqing) There was fierce fighting on the front lines the day before yesterday. The bandits retreated dozens of li. There is a rumor that Songkan has been recovered. The Central Army in northern Guizhou is in close pursuit of the bandits, who have withdrawn a portion of their forces from Tongzi and Songkan to defend the rear. It is currently unlikely that they will flee to Sichuan. (20th Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Hankou) Wang Youyong, the director of the Second Department of the General Staff, will fly to Chongqing on the 21st after completing his official business in Hankou. He Chengjun will also go after meeting with Chiang Kai-shek. (20th Dispatch)

Liu Xiang's Representative Arrived in Shaanxi 22

To Discuss the Military Suppression of Bandits in Northern Sichuan

(Xi'an) Liu Xiang's representative Wang Yunzi arrived in Xi'an by train on the evening of the 19th to meet with Yang Hucheng to discuss the military suppression of bandits in northern Sichuan. According to Wang, he will meet with Hu Zongnan in Tianshui after meeting with Yang in Xi'an, and then return to Chongqing to report back. The Sichuan bandits in northern Sichuan have been blockaded by our army and have no power to develop. The bandits who fled to Sichuan from Guizhou will find it difficult to cross the Yangtze River. All sectors of Sichuan Province welcome the Shaanxi and Gansu armies to enter Sichuan to cooperate in the suppression, to relieve the people from their suffering. The fates of Sichuan, Shaanxi, and Gansu are closely related, and it is hoped that they will help each other. (20th Central News Agency Dispatch)

International Press Corps Arrived in Nancheng Yesterday for Inspection 23

(Nanchang) The international press corps, led by Xiao Chunjin, a member of the provincial government, and Huang Chaoqin, a section chief of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, departed from the provincial government at 8:00 AM on the 20th in 15 buses from the Highway Bureau to inspect the newly recovered areas. They are scheduled to spend the night in Nancheng. According to a phone call from Linchuan, the press corps passed through Linchuan at 12:30 PM without stopping and went directly to Nancheng. According to a phone call from Nancheng, the group arrived in Nancheng at 2:00 PM. The administrative commissioner Zhang Xie accompanied them to the station to welcome them. After lunch at Commander-in-Chief Chiang Kai-shek's Nancheng headquarters, they transferred to the service area of the Economic Commission in Xinfeng Town, which is 40 li from Nancheng, for a visit. They returned to Nancheng at 8:30 PM and stayed at the headquarters. Seeing the bunkers along the way, the reporters deeply admired the people's efforts to assist in the suppression of bandits. Seeing the greatness of the highway project, they also praised it. (20th Central Dispatch)

Military Vehicles Collided in Zhangzhou 24

(Xiamen) A military vehicle and a transportation vehicle of the 80th Division collided in Zhangzhou, injuring nine officers and soldiers and killing one orderly. (20th Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Xiamen) 334 Min籍 soldiers from Guangdong arrived at Xiamen on the Fu'an warship and were transferred to the Pacification Commissioner's Office for disposal. (20th Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Xiamen) The Pacification Commissioner's Office stationed in Fujian dispatched troops from the 1st Security Regiment to maintain traffic on the Quanzhou-Xiamen road. (20th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Lin Yunhai Resigned as Chairman of Guangdong Provincial Government 25

(Hong Kong) Lin Yunhai resigned as Chairman of the Guangdong Provincial Government to the Political Council. The Political Council persuaded him to stay, but Lin's determination to resign was extremely firm. Chen Jitang plans to appoint Xiang Hanping as the mayor of Guangzhou. Li Yangjing returned to the province from Huiyang on the 19th and is scheduled to go to the military academy on the 21st. (20th Dispatch)

(Hong Kong) The Guangdong Provincial Assembly is scheduled to hold its second meeting on February 15th, and proposals must be submitted within five days. (20th Dispatch)

(Hong Kong) After arriving in Liuzhou, the Second Army of Guangdong will be under the command of Li Bai. (20th Dispatch)

Beijing Municipal Money Industry Concluding Period 26

(Nanjing) Beijing Municipal Money Industry follows the Chamber of Commerce's order to use the Gregorian calendar for the year-end conclusion. Because most stores are accustomed to the old habits, silver and money collection and delivery cannot be completed until the end of the lunar year. According to information from the money industry, the date of general collection and delivery for the money shops in the city has been set for February 3, which is the 30th day of the twelfth lunar month. They will close for four days from the 4th and begin operations on the 8th. According to past practice, most stores plan to close on the 5th day of the lunar new year for the God of Wealth wine. Some will close for five days. (20th Dispatch)

Postal Directorate General's Relocation to Nanjing Largely Completed 27

(Nanjing) The relocation of the Postal Directorate General to Nanjing has been largely completed by the 20th. Director Guo Xinzhong arrived in Nanjing on the morning of the 20th and personally went to the new site to plan everything. All employees will come to Nanjing in batches on the 20th and 21st and will report to the new bureau on the 21st. It is reported that operations in Nanjing can begin on the 2nd or 12th. (20th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Capital to Commemorate Chen Shaobai Today 28

(Nanjing) Chen Shaobai's memorial service is scheduled to be held at the Jinghua Overseas Chinese Guest House in Beijing at 2:00 PM on the 21st. Preparations and arrangements were completed on the 20th. The elegiac couplets given by various Central Committee members and various agencies have reached more than 100 pieces. The Central Executive and Supervisory Committee presented a horizontal plaque with the eight characters "He is a pioneer of the people of heaven," which is hung in the center of the memorial hall. The chief officiant of the memorial service will be determined by the Standing Committee, and all Central Committee members in Nanjing will participate. (20th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Judicial Yuan Clarifies Questions on the Calculation of the Judgment Period 29

(Nanjing) The Judicial Yuan decided to interpret the ambiguities regarding the calculation of the judgment confirmation period as meaning that all second-instance judgments exceeding 300 yuan shall be deemed confirmed at the time of the judgment if the parties have not applied for special appeal or if the original court has rejected their application. (20th Dispatch)

Chen Daqi Talks About Examination Work 30

(Nanjing) Chen Daqi, Chairman of the Examination Commission, said that this year's work will include holding a central higher examination once and a general examination in all provinces once. According to the original regulations, the higher examination is held once every two years, with the next session in September. The Higher Examination Law is still pending revision, so the date has not been determined. It will be held in four districts: Beijing, Ping, Guangdong, and Shaanxi. As for the general examination, the provinces have not fully complied with holding it. The Examination Yuan will issue an order to all provincial governments that they must hold a general examination once this year, regardless of whether they have already held it or not. It is also not yet determined whether the Central Government will hold a general examination this year. If the central agencies can comply with the resolutions of the Examination and Assessment Conference and eliminate a few percent of their staff, then there will be a need to hold one to fill the vacancies; otherwise, it will not be necessary. (20th Dispatch)

National Treasury Branch's Copper Seal Made 31

(Nanjing) The copper seals for the National Treasury and its branches in various locations have been made by the Seal Casting Bureau. The National Government has recently sent them to the Executive Yuan for distribution. (20th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Tax Police Corps Transferred to Haizhou 32

(Nanjing) The task of suppressing bandits in Jiangxi by the Tax Police Corps of the Ministry of Finance has ended. They have been transferred to Haizhou to resume their original defense duties and to take on the task of salt smuggling suppression. The 2nd and 3rd Regiments have passed through Beiping to the north, and the 4th Regiment and directly subordinate battalions and companies will continue to move to Haizhou from Beijing on the 20th. (20th Central News Agency Dispatch)

National Government Commends Ye Ziheng and Others 33

Liu Hongsheng Discusses the Future of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Business 38

(Nanjing) Liu Hongsheng arrived in Nanjing to discuss the reorganization of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company. Old docks and cargo-handling machines were repaired, and old ships were put back into service. Currently, cargo transport on the Yangtze River is congested, and warehouses are full. Business between Guangzhou and Hong Kong is also good, and intermodal transport is particularly frequent. Last year's operating revenue and expenditure were balanced, with a surplus. However, the repayment of old debts and interest is too large, so we can only勉付子息, and we are still unable to use the surplus to expand business. In the past, in order to expand long-distance routes, we planned to raise 10 million in shipping industry bonds, which is still under review by the Ministry of Finance and the Economic Council. After careful discussion, we plan to issue it to add new ships, because the Nanyang route requires new ships to open up. The shipping industry cooperation association has been established, and the shipping industry will be more stable than the current free competition in the future, and the occurrence of dangerous accidents in adventurous voyages can be reduced. The result of free competition is that each route used to require the deployment of ten ships to and from each other. Now, due to the lack of restrictions, it has increased to more than ten ships, which is not in accordance with economic principles and leads to losses. In addition, due to greedy loading exceeding the deadweight tonnage, sinking has occurred. Now, each route is equipped according to the needs of passengers and cargo, and the remaining ships are repaired and new routes are opened up. Cooperation is the most important condition for alleviating the current economic downturn in various industries, and it is also the newest method of this century. Finally, it is said that all the stocks have been repurchased, and what remains is probably only the lost part. (20th Special Telegram)

Current Commentary

New Trends in the World Political Situation Shu 41

Over the past year, the European continent has accumulated various dangerous materials. If not handled carefully, they could trigger a global upheaval. Issues such as Austria's independence, the deteriorating relations between Italy and Southern Europe, and the confrontation between France and Germany all contain the crisis of war. Once erupted, they would have broad global implications. In the Pacific, since Japan unilaterally declared the abolition of the naval treaty, the arms race between the United States and Japan and the various disputes between Japan and the Soviet Union have intensified. How the future will unfold is hard to be optimistic.

Unexpectedly, at the beginning of this year, after the French Foreign Minister visited Rome, France and Italy reached an understanding. France made concessions to Italy in Tunisia and ceded 80,000 square miles of North African territory to Italy. At the same time, it also recognized joint management with Italy of railways in its布基.阿基.阿白巴. Moreover, the exchange obtained is primarily a Central European peace treaty, linking Austria-Hungary, Czechoslovakia, Yugoslavia, Poland, Romania, and other countries into one entity, to be jointly negotiated by France and Italy to ensure Austria's independence. In other words, it is a renewed formation of an alliance surrounding Germany. This can be described as a special gain in diplomacy outside of conferences, and also a sign of a turning point in the global situation.

As for the crisis in Western Europe, the Saar issue is the most likely to trigger a major change. France also knows that争彼区区administrative power benefits France very little. It only causes displeasure for both Britain and Italy and easily provokes opposition from the Germans. The wisest countermeasure is to follow the results of local people's votes to determine who the administrative power belongs to. Moreover, France still retains the right to coal and iron ore deposits in the Saar mining area. Germany must prepare 300 million to 400 million gold francs as the price to acquire the mining rights. It is not without benefit to France. Therefore, France treats the Saar vote calmly and without any difficulties. Germany can also slightly ease its resentment and may be able to return to the League of Nations to engage in compromise at the conference table and return to peace. This matter is not only that France can take the overall situation into consideration, but also that Britain is working hard. According to the国民社 on the 19th, the Lord Privy Seal of the United Kingdom, Eden, delivered a speech on the Saar vote, saying, "Britain's policy towards Europe is only to seek a deeper friendship with neighboring countries. The resolution of this Saar vote allows us to hope that a new era of compromise has begun. If all countries want to go further, take advantage of the opportunity to achieve concrete results, they should cooperate and not just talk. In order to ensure Europe once and for all, we will cooperate more closely in the coming months. This is the key to maintaining lasting peace." From this speech, it can be seen that the European situation has prospects for improvement.

Since the end of last year, the United States has been agitated by the Pacific tide and deeply feels that international problems are not easy to deal with. Therefore, it has decided to join the International Court of Justice. Judging from the current international situation, this move may not have any effect, but for the United States, in this era of evolution, it is difficult to stick to its views and refuse to be imprisoned. The United States' joining the International Court of Justice has added a lot of luster to the League of Nations. After the preliminary meeting on naval reduction formed a deadlock, Britain and the United States gradually approached each other and jointly advocated their actual shipbuilding power in order to establish an appropriate arms reduction treaty before 1936. If there are no unexpected obstacles, this de facto understanding of naval reduction can be formed. Then, there is also a glimmer of hope for peace in the Far East.

However, this kind of understanding on arms reduction is only limited to a part of the scope of arms reduction. There are many hidden reefs in other overall political issues. To remove these obstacles, the first requirement is that strong countries in the Far East can deeply realize the necessity of maintaining peace and that the policy of aggression is not suitable for today's world. Only then can there be hope for peace. Otherwise, although the European situation has seen a relaxation, and the League of Nations has increased its strength due to the accession of the Soviet Union, the understanding between Italy and France, and the expression of goodwill from the United States, what methods can be used to deal with the Far East?

Three Uninhabited Pacific Islands Transferred to US Navy Department for Management 42

The reason is unknown, or a flight training ground may be built.

No contact has been made on the issue of Japanese-administered islands.

(Washington) Three uninhabited islands in the Pacific Ocean were transferred to the direct jurisdiction of the US Navy Department today. The reasons have not been announced. These three islands are quite close to Hawaii: Wake Island, Kingman Reef, and Johnston Atoll. (19th Reuters Telegram)

(Washington) President Roosevelt, with the special permission of Congress, today transferred Wake Island, Kingman Reef, Johnston Island, and Sand Island (except for Wake Island, the other three islands belong to the Hawaiian Islands) to the jurisdiction of the Navy Department. It is learned that this move is in preparation to temporarily use Wake Island as a Pacific airfield for the planned Sino-US Pacific aviation. (19th国民电)

(Washington) President Roosevelt announced today the transfer of Wake and other islands to the jurisdiction of the Navy Department. At the same time, the press also asked Secretary of State Hull about the US attitude regarding the fact that the League of Nations Administrative Council still recognized the Pacific trust islands as being under Japanese rule. He replied that the United States had not exchanged views with any country on this matter and that the government had no opinion to express on the actions of the League of Nations Administrative Council at this time. It is generally believed that the United States is temporarily unwilling to intervene in this matter, but still retains the right to jointly deal with the Pacific trust islands as stipulated in the Treaty of Versailles. According to what the Secretary of State said, this statement has been confirmed. (19th国民电)

(Geneva) The League of Nations Committee on Mandates issued a report on the meeting of the Committee in October and November of last year on the 4th of this month, stating that Japan had spent huge sums of money building ports in the Pacific mandate islands, which was not commensurate with the commercial needs there. This report has recently been passed by the League of Nations Administrative Council, but it did not mention Japan or the issue of the Pacific mandate islands after Japan's withdrawal from the League of Nations. It is generally recognized that after Japan's withdrawal from the League of Nations in March of this year, Japan will continue to occupy the mandate islands. However, this is inevitable and not due to the decision of the League of Nations Administrative Council. (19th哈瓦斯电)

New Army Aviation Regulations in the US 43

(Washington) The Army Department today promulgated newly revised Army Aviation Regulations. If strictly enforced, the days when general aviation officers sit comfortably in swivel chairs and never take off will soon be over. According to the newly revised regulations, all aviation personnel with more than fifteen years of service must prove their flying ability every year in order to continue serving in the aviation team. And they must fly at least one hundred hours in various weather conditions each year. If they fail the annual exam or do not have enough flying time, they must be transferred back to the ground force to serve. Observers familiar with the aviation situation believe that this regulation will greatly help both the effectiveness and morale of the aviation team. The officials at all levels of the aviation team have long been unable to fly. It is recalled that General Mitchell of the aviation team also advocated this plan many years ago. However, after he exposed the corruption of the aviation personnel, he was squeezed out by his colleagues, and even allowed to choose between resigning or being suspended for five years. At that time, Mitchell resigned on his own. However, attacks on the lack of effectiveness of the aviation team have not stopped. Moreover, this move by the Army Department is in line with the attitude of President Roosevelt and his government advisors, who advocate that the Army Department's grade-by-grade promotion system should be abolished, and that the Army should learn from the Navy to improve its effectiveness. (19th国民电)

US Senator Advocates Silver Standard 44

(Washington) Democratic Congressman Dai Martin said in an interview with the Associated Press today that he supports the single silver standard and that the old Spanish silver dollar, containing 412.5 英釐 of silver, should be the unit of currency. Dai also said that this measure would be the most effective way to raise prices and reduce the burden of debt, and that a future international bimetallic standard would be feasible. Dai believes that the instability of international exchange rates can be avoided because the Ministry of Finance can still store huge amounts of cash to regulate exchange rates. Now he will propose that exports and agricultural products can be given price premiums with silver, and he has strongly urged the Ministry of Finance to continue its silver purchase plan, while trying to reconcile the conflicting interests of China and the United States. Dai continued, "Gold is no longer sufficient as a medium of exchange, and its main use is only for clearing international differences and for storage. Since we currently have no gold standard, I propose a silver standard. The value of the dollar remains the same. In this way, we can use silver as the standard and gold as the reserve, and credit can be stabilized accordingly. International commercial competition will make other countries accept this standard. Moreover, this move is not expansion, but just a change of standard. Prices do not have to risk issuing paper money to be raised. In fact, we have abolished the gold standard, but all prices in the United States are still based on gold dollars. If they are changed to silver coins, all debts can be easily cleared, and other countries' debts to the United States can also be easily repaid." Dai believes that if the world's existing gold reserves can be distributed evenly and all man-made trade barriers are removed, then maintaining the gold standard is also possible. However, gold-holding countries are determined not to redistribute, and lending is also difficult under the current circumstances. There are no difficulties in the distribution of silver, because the world's silver reserves are twelve times more than gold, and the amount of silver produced annually can still be increased. Therefore, Dai believes that if the Supreme Court does not allow the revocation of the "gold payment clause", the United States will have to collect silver at a premium, or allow foreign merchants to enjoy a 40% advantage over US importers and exporters. (19th国民电)

(Washington) Today, the nine justices of the Supreme Court held an informal meeting in a secret room of Congress to negotiate the judgment on the lawsuit filed by Norman against the government. Therefore, Roosevelt's monetary policy of abolishing the 1933 gold clause is in danger of being shaken. The court may decide on an opinion on Monday of next week, and then write an opinion. It is expected that a final decision will not be made before February 4. The question to be decided now is whether the government's suspension of the gold payment clause is constitutional. If the court's ruling is unfavorable to the government, then the government's payment of bonds worth 169,000,000,000 yuan with the currently devalued US dollar will be significantly affected. (19th Reuters Telegram)

Billions of pounds of current assets are idle

Millions of people are unemployed

(London) Former British wartime Prime Minister Lloyd George delivered his second speech today in Baoxi里 on a new plan to alleviate the economic difficulties of Britain. There were many listeners, saying that Britain is real. The machines are rusty and urgently need to be wiped and lubricated to make them operate smoothly. George repeatedly stated that his proposals were completely non-partisan. What he seeks is more efficient industry, more fertile soil, happier families and a more equal distribution of human happiness. Now, no less than billions of pounds of current assets are idled in banks and do not circulate, and millions of people are wandering the streets without work. We should pay attention to this and remedy the country's shortcomings. If we do so, Britain will be encouraged by the vision and measures of its rulers. (19th Reuters Telegram)

Place Europe in a Realm of Lasting Peace

(Geneva) British Lord Privy Seal Eden delivered a broadcast speech on the Saar vote, saying, "Britain's policy towards Europe is only to seek a deeper friendship with neighboring countries. The resolution of this Saar vote allows us to hope that a new era of compromise has begun. If all countries want to go further, take advantage of the opportunity to achieve concrete results, they should cooperate and not just talk. For the sake of Europe once and for all, all countries should cooperate closely in the coming months, as this is the key to maintaining lasting peace." (19th国民电)

(Berlin) The Berliner Tageblatt refuted the claims in French newspapers that a large number of residents were fleeing the Saar region, saying that the so-called number of migrants reaching 20,000 to 45,000 was exaggerated. According to recent reports, only more than 700 residents of the Saar have left the Saar for France so far, which can be divided into two parts. One part is those who went to the Saar to seek jobs from the诺克斯 or the separatist faction, and the rest are only a few thousand people. The newspaper also said that the reason why France is 悻悻 is that these people will have no place to settle after arriving in France. However, when they were in the Saar, they only served France. It is inappropriate for France to say that they should be responsible by the League of Nations because they voted to maintain the status quo. But who is responsible has nothing to do with Germany. (19th国民电)

(Berlin) Will Germany's foreign policy change due to the return of the Saar region? This question is quite interesting. Since the results of the plebiscite were announced, people from all walks of life in Berlin were full of optimism, and Hitler, "Leader and Chancellor," gave a radio speech on the day of the announcement, saying that Germany no longer had any territorial demands on France. After this statement, the optimistic mood became even more certain. However, the German media has repeatedly demonstrated against France and the League of Nations, and their rhetoric has become impatient. In addition, after Hitler delivered two important speeches, the optimism of the general public had to be greatly reduced. In short, Germany's position was revealed by Hitler tomorrow. The saying that territorial demands were given up has been around since the Treaty of Locarno was signed and is not a new political factor. Hitler's meaning is that Germany's concessions have stopped here, and other countries cannot make any more demands. If so, then what he said earlier was only to create an atmosphere, and it cannot be regarded as a concrete embodiment of Germany's future foreign policy. For the sake of the stability of the European situation, it would be very beneficial if Germany could return to Geneva. However, Hitler seems to have indicated that various disarmament restrictions are rejected in principle. If Germany wants to adopt diplomatic promises, the only condition is to clearly recognize Germany's rearmament as legal, which is a pity. As for Germany's position on the Eastern European Mutual Assistance Pact, it has now clearly changed. Hitler's declaration contained the only concrete proposal, that he was prepared to sign a non-aggression treaty with France, which was no different from the one Germany signed with Poland on January 26 last year. Mr. Hitler also declared clearly that he was not very interested in the League of Nations. This is also reflected in Berlin, where the current situation is beneficial to Germany and does no harm. Germany can actually recognize that it is not bound by the Treaty of Versailles and actively rearm itself. This is to express the honor and equal rights of the German nation. (19th哈瓦斯电)

After the Saar Issue is Resolved, Germany Wants Memel Again 49

Newspapers Begin to Criticize Lithuania

(Berlin) Since the Saar issue was resolved, Germany's vision has shifted to the east, as evidenced by the recent criticism by some German newspapers of Lithuania's deployment of troops in Memel. Memel has an area of 943 square miles and a population of 146,000. On February 16, 1923, it was incorporated into Lithuanian territory. National Political Party Convention: Machida Inaugurated as President 51

(Tokyo) This afternoon at 1 PM, the National Political Party held a convention at the Ueno Seiyōken. Former President Wakatsuki delivered a speech, after which Raimaki Keikichi gave a thank-you speech to the former president. Subsequently, new staff and declarations were decided. Finally, the new President Machida delivered a speech and the meeting adjourned. The inaugural speech of the new President Machida is as follows: When President Wakatsuki resigned, based on the resolution of the joint meeting of party members and councilors, President Wakatsuki designated a successor. Although I firmly declined, the party's situation could not allow for a prolonged vacancy in the presidency. After the persistent requests of the former president, executives, and party members, I reluctantly accepted this difficult task. I earnestly request the assistance of all party members. Although our party has been a minority party in recent years, it has gained trust, entirely due to the appropriate handling by the former president. Therefore, I deeply appreciate his achievements during his tenure. However, my talent is limited, and my knowledge is shallow. I hope for guidance and encouragement from senior members. Therefore, I plan to recommend Wakatsuki, Yamamoto, Taketomi Tokitoshi, and Katō Masayoshi as Supreme Advisors. The new staff is as follows: Secretaries-General: Ōta Masahiro, Ogawa Gōtarō, Ōasa Tadao, Katsuta Eikichi, Raimaki Keikichi (Chief Secretary), Taketomi Watanabe, Tanaka Takeo, Nakajima Yadanji, Umezawa Uyahachi, Uchisaki Sakuzaburō. Negotiations on the Chinese Eastern Railway 52

(Tokyo) The third round of detailed negotiations regarding the Chinese Eastern Railway this year has been ongoing since the 17th. From 4 PM on the 19th, Tōgō, the Director of the Eurasian Bureau, and Representative Kaslovsky met at the Ministry of Foreign Affairs until 11:30 PM, discussing for over seven hours. They discussed the unresolved issues from the previous meeting, such as the price determination and the insertion of arbitration clauses in case of contract breach, as well as the calculation method for the payment of pensions to bureau staff and all other issues. Both sides engaged in enthusiastic negotiations. As a result of the above discussions, a complete consensus has not yet been reached regarding the insertion of arbitration clauses. As for other details, some technical considerations still remain. However, the main points of the transfer negotiations have largely reached agreement between the two sides. The representatives will meet with Director Tōgō again next Monday or Tuesday, at which time the issues should be resolved. The negotiations on the 19th have virtually concluded the details. If progress continues smoothly, a committee to draft the agreement documents can be established within the next week. The drafting of these clauses will take about a month. It is estimated that the signing of the agreement will take place in early March. (20th, Nichen Telegram)

Spanish Aviator Plans to Explore the Stratosphere 53

Madrid: Major Emilio Herrera, a famous Spanish aviator, will conduct an unprecedented exploration of the stratosphere in early February. The equipment used for this ascent will be an ordinary balloon and an open gondola. Major Herrera enjoys a long-standing reputation in the aviation world and is a frequent passenger on Zeppelins. He also has a considerable position in the scientific community. This daring adventure is worthy of worldwide attention. Herrera has been preparing tirelessly for the past eighteen months. The balloon used for the ascent has a hydrogen capacity of 1,600 cubic meters. At its highest altitude, its diameter will be 36 meters. The most important part of the balloon, which is related to the success of the trip, is the balloon box. This box was custom-made in Germany. The remaining parts, including the gondola, were specially manufactured by the Guadarrama military aircraft factory near the Spanish capital. Previous stratosphere explorations have all used sealed golden gondolas to carry people, isolating the internal and external air. However, the current gondola is open, so preparations must be meticulous and thorough. It is reported that Herrera will use a self-heated electric swimming suit to maintain body temperature. Inside the swimming suit, he will wear a specially made object made of steel wire, which is extremely strong. Inside this object, he will then wear two special sets of underwear, one made of rubber, which is waterproof, and one made of wool. In addition, there will be an oxygen tank for breathing en route. Currently, Herrera is practicing navigation at the Madrid Industrial School every day. The school has prepared a special test chamber, where the temperature is constantly at 60 degrees Celsius or 66 degrees below zero Fahrenheit, which is the estimated temperature at an altitude of 20,000 meters. The suitability of the clothes and equipment will be determined in this test chamber. Herrera estimates that ascent and descent will each take two hours. A small compartment will be used for high-altitude observation. The planned altitude is 23,000 meters. If this altitude can be reached, all previous records will be broken. Professor Picard of Belgium's highest record is 16,200 meters. Later, American scientists ascended to 18,665 meters. Soviet scientists ascended to 22,000 meters. However, the Soviet scientists did not survive. Herrera plans to ascend alone. However, his wife does not want her husband to risk such a great danger alone and asked to accompany him. However, Herrera said that adding one person to the balloon would reduce the altitude by at least 1,000 meters, so he does not want her to go. Herrera will carry a short-wave radio transmitter with him to report observations at any time en route. The most interesting aspect of this ascent is that when the balloon reaches an altitude of 20,000 meters, the entire Iberian Peninsula will be visible at once. Herrera plans to use the method of analyzing external light to capture a panoramic view of Spain and Portugal at that time. If successful, the entire map of a country will be captured on camera for the first time. (18th, Guomin Telegram)

French Trade Decreases Significantly 54

Progress in European Rural Areas 60

(Berlin Correspondence) Since the Great War, all industries in Europe have been devastated, especially in Germany. However, Germany has returned to normal in the shortest possible time. The issue of rural revival is another serious event in Europe. The reporter interviewed Dr. Winter, the leading cadre of the German National Food Office, to inquire about the rural issues in Europe. I was granted an interview. A record of his conversation is as follows:

At present, the desire of all countries in the world to revive world trade is becoming stronger, while at the same time, the restrictions on international commodity transactions are also becoming increasingly strict. It seems that people do not pay deep attention to this. The solution to this difficulty is the new German land distribution policy. We must first study the concept of European farmers. What exactly is it? In fact, the European countries are economically and internationally interdependent. Under this kind of situation, only by jointly cooperating to use the advantages of each nation to obtain profits can the state of their poverty be slightly reduced. This is indeed an economic problem of increasing national consumption capacity.

Europe has no new strategies for the farmers themselves. The old ideas, such as when the British Minister of Agriculture, Cromwell (a leader of the Republican Party), initiated the World Colonial Council, were extinguished after the French Revolution. At that time, economic competition was the beginning of general market hostility, and the fact that rural areas were the foundation of the economy was forgotten and no longer considered. Today, when we consider it carefully, we know that it was a mistake. For example, it was unbelievable to people at that time that the US President would intervene in wheat matters not long ago. Therefore, it is clear that directly resolving economic problems is impossible. Today, the thinking of European farmers is in the process of revival. The basis of its new thinking is the German government's agricultural land policy. Farmers must first have firmness and security in order to generate basic concepts.

German leader Hitler and Minister of Agriculture Ganli have formulated laws on agricultural product markets in order to achieve this goal. These laws are not only implemented in one's own country, but can also be used in trade between countries, because the true nature of commodity transactions should be in firmness and not speculation, which leads to fluctuations. Farmers are very clear about this point.

The goal of the German market laws is not limited to one's own country, and the German Ministry of Agriculture can thereby improve the living standards and consumption capacity of European farmers. European industry will also gradually become vibrant because of this. The formulation of these economic laws is not only implemented on Germany's agricultural product imports, but also equally applied to Germany's exports to European countries.

Europe's concept of farmers arises from the assumption that European countries still have unlimited purchasing potential. This concept has now become a reality. The goal of Germany's commercial policy is to "increase trade mutual assistance." Generally speaking, this plan can only be successful on the basis of the new land distribution law. The market law is sufficient to control foreign imports and protect domestic production prices from the impact of commodity imports. Regarding agricultural products, the government has established agencies to manage all imports and ensure the stability of imported commodities. At present, the Netherlands and Denmark, Hungary and Switzerland, Finland and Yugoslavia, have all formed commercial treaties based on this. The success of this farmer-to-farmer treaty has also made Europe's thinking on farmers a reality. In the next few years, it will not be a problem for Europe to conclude such trade treaties internationally. Germany is very satisfied with the implementation of the above policies. Its success in increasing imports and agricultural products will be enough to make all countries recognize Germany as a loyal customer. (Guomin News Agency)

The German National Socialist Party's Agricultural Control (German Correspondence) 81

The Truth About the National Food Corporation

Strengthening Dictatorial Agricultural Policies

"More important than anything else is the great integration of the economy, that is, the integration of a production sector within the entire German economy." This is what Dr. Wattadaler, the Minister of Food, said. His main idea is to unite agricultural workers, landlords, etc., to form large cartels and trusts similar to various organizations in industry. He believes that a cartel of agricultural products can definitely be realized. This is also because of Germany's current economic difficulties. Export trade cannot move forward, and there are no colonial markets for development, so it is necessary to find ways to develop the domestic market and break through towards a controlled economy. Since September 1933, the National Socialist Party has been working to realize its ideal of controlling agriculture. The first step was to organize the "National Food Corporation." This organization, with Food Minister Dahle as its supreme leader, forcibly included all agricultural entrepreneurs, owner-farmers, tenant farmers, farm laborers, rural cooperatives, merchants selling agricultural products, agricultural product processors, etc. Members of the National Food Corporation must absolutely obey the leadership of their leaders, otherwise they will be severely punished. As for those involved in guiding policies, they are large landlords, large agricultural capitalists, or large wholesalers related to agricultural products. Therefore, the power of the Food Minister has increased, and the power of influential figures in agriculture in general has also increased. This is very similar to the cartels in industry.

The law on controlling grains was promulgated in September 1933. First, the Minister of Food has the power to control the production price and the sales price of grains. According to this law, the Minister of Food can determine the market price of wheat and rye. This is what grain producers must abide by when they first take grains to the market for sale. He divides the entire Germany into nine districts, each with price differences based on its geographical conditions, and gradually increases the prices. By June of this year, the wheat price had increased by 12% and the rye price had increased by 7%. No other prices are allowed for market transactions outside of these prices, and speculative transactions such as forward trading are not allowed. If such transactions are made, the government will impose severe penalties. Second, the Minister of Food has the power to order the combination of flour companies and may prohibit them from new equipment and expansion of the business. According to this law, an economic union of wheat and rye is organized with all flour mills in Germany as members. The main tasks of the union are: (1) to limit the expansion of existing production equipment, and (2) to order each operator to produce in proportion based on the average production volume.

Understanding the above situation, we can know that the main purpose of its control is: first, to maintain the price of wheat, and second, to limit the supply of flour, maintain the price of flour, so that this industrial sector of Germany is not agitated by market trends, and the people's food source is also more stably guaranteed.

After June 1934, due to the control of grains, the power of the Minister of Food exceeded the original power. He can control the sales methods and the quantity of sales of grains, and can also control the purchase of raw materials and the sale of manufactured products by grain merchants, flour enterprises, etc. In other words, the Minister has the right to decide the amount of flour produced by flour mills and the amount of bread produced by bakeries. Therefore, the grain price determined by the Minister of Food in the second half of this year is very different from the price determined at the same time last year. Last year, the price determined was the minimum price, and this year it is a buying and selling price. There is not much profit for the merchants in between. Now the whole Germany is divided into nineteen districts, and each district has organized a "Grain Economic Group." These economic groups are united to form the "German Grain Economic Central Union." The union directs the local areas, and the Minister of Food is in the position of supervisor.

Not only grains, but also milk and other agricultural products are organized in a similar way to establish the local economic groups and central alliances to determine sales areas and market prices. The situation of agricultural control in Germany is roughly like this. (December 20 in Berlin)
