The second batch of delegates arrived in Xun on the morning of the 18th by the Datong Wheel and then transferred to a passenger train in the afternoon to the south. They arrived at Niuhang Station at around 9 p.m. and were also received by the reception staff to stay at the reception center.

Visiting the Suburbs 88

After having lunch at the reception center, the delegation visited Ping'anbao, Qingyunpu, the Martyrs' Cemetery, Lintang Rural Normal School, and the Agricultural College in the suburbs, accompanied by various reception staff. They returned to the province at 6 p.m. At 7 p.m., they attended a banquet hosted by the Municipal Committee. Director Gong Xuesui of the committee first invited them to visit for a week, and then sat down and chatted for a while at the city's Guang Club before entering the city's Guang Canteen for dinner. During the banquet, Director Gong gave a welcome speech and reported on the construction of the province and the city and the general situation of the city's administration. Xia Xieqiang and others translated it into English and Japanese. The guests and hosts enjoyed themselves until 9 p.m.

Gong's Speech 89

The arrival of this international press delegation in Nanchang is truly a grand event. On behalf of the 260,000 citizens, I would like to express my welcome. I am deeply honored that you gentlemen have graced us with your presence at the Municipal Committee's banquet tonight. I would like to take this opportunity to briefly report on the construction of Jiangxi and the municipal administration of this city. 1. Construction of Jiangxi: Since the establishment of the Republic of China, this province has set up an agency in charge of the province's industrial and administrative affairs. The matters handled include rural areas, water conservancy, fisheries and animal husbandry, cultivation, industry and commerce, mining administration, municipal administration, transportation, mass organizations, labor-capital arbitration, and cooperatives. Its affiliated agencies have successively set up a highway office, a water conservancy bureau, a ceramics experimental institute, an industrial experimental institute, a geological and mining survey institute, a livelihood factory, a measurement and testing institute, a Pingxiang coal mine, a management office, and a construction bank, etc. Because the government attaches special importance to various undertakings, it specially established a rural cooperative committee three years ago to share the responsibility of rural cooperative undertakings with the Construction Department. Also, because of the emphasis on agriculture and forestry, an agricultural college was established a year ago, and the two farms in Nanchang and Hukou, and the three forest farms in Lushan Pengze and Jingdezhen, which were formerly under the jurisdiction of the Construction Department, were transferred to the Agricultural College and are now actively underway. Among the construction projects in this province in the past three years, the most noteworthy is the highway. To date, there are nearly 5,000 kilometers of highways that can be opened to traffic. This achievement is due to the voluntary service of the people and the enthusiastic participation of the army. The issue of vehicles traveling on the highways is now under study. Starting this year, we plan to use the people's habit of building roads to engage in water conservancy construction, such as dredging rivers, repairing embankments, digging ditches and ponds, etc. This plan will be completed in six years. Several months of labor will be requisitioned each year, totaling approximately 10 million workers. In addition, there are also development plans for local products in this province, such as porcelain, tea, paper, summer cloth, and鵭 mines. We are preparing to carry them out separately. 2. Municipal administration of this city: Jiangxi is an agricultural society, so it did not pay much attention to municipal administration in the past. The old urban area was only more than 26,350 mu (each mu is equal to 666 meters). Since the establishment of the Republic of China, transportation and industry and commerce have gradually developed, and the population of Nanchang has gradually increased. It was not until the revolutionary army arrived in Nanchang in the 15th year of the Republic of China that a municipal administration agency was established to dismantle the city walls and open up roads. Since last year, various municipal construction works have become more active. In short, they are as follows: (1) Reorganizing land and expanding the urban area: The land in the old urban area will be measured in detail, a 1/500 map will be made, private land will be registered separately, and household maps will be issued. At the same time, the urban area will be expanded tenfold. (2) Water supply and drainage facilities: The citizens of this city use river water as drinking water. A water filtration station was set up a year ago, which provides an average of 100,000 gallons of clean water to the citizens every day. Now we want to use 1.4 million yuan to open a water plant, which can produce 250,000 gallons of clean water per hour. As for the drainage facilities, there were originally very good ditches. Recently, due to the demolition of the city and the construction of roads, the drainage system is bound to change. The East Lake has now been dredged. According to the entire plan, water pipes will be installed. The drainage problem can be completely solved within two years. (3) Electric lights and telephones: The electric lights in this city were formerly run by merchants. The municipal administration agency temporarily took over the management a year ago. The old design was 1KW. Now we are adding 1KW and preparing to allocate another 1.8 million yuan to build a new power plant with three WK generators. In addition to electric lights, it will also supply industrial power. The telephones in this city were also originally run by merchants. Last year, the Ministry of Communications set up a telephone bureau to improve the telephones in this city. A communications building is now being built to move the three parts of telephone, telegraph, and post office into one building to facilitate the citizens. (4) Others: More than 300 mu of new residential areas have been opened up, and another 200 mu are now being expanded. One hundred buildings of public housing have been built, most of which have been completed. The ones currently being planned are the Confucius Temple, Tengwang Pavilion, the Bandit Suppression Memorial Hall, ten guild halls, a women's club, and five public bathhouses, as well as the reconstruction of the city's elementary schools. Regarding transportation, the roads are being widened and the Zhongzheng Bridge is being built to connect the transportation on both sides of the Gan River. In short, Jiangxi is bound to have a dilapidated appearance everywhere after being ravaged by the Communists. However, we believe that the Communists can destroy, we can build, the Communists destroy quickly, and we build even faster. The vigor of those in charge and the two hands of the common people are the driving force for building a new Jiangxi. Finally, I would like to toast this glass to the health of everyone. (Central News Agency, January 18)

Yellow River Commission Plans to Formulate Ice Prevention and Guidance Measures 90

Personnel Sent to Qinghe Town Longmen for Inspection

Kaifeng Correspondence: The Yellow River Water Conservancy Commission believes that the Yellow River's ice run is very important because it affects river engineering. First, wherever the ice goes, dams and slopes are damaged, and the amount of石料 lost each year is very large. Second, because the ice blocks the water, the water will rise, leading to overflowing embankments and breaches. Now that the ice season is approaching, ice has begun to flow in the Tongguan and Shaanxi areas since the beginning of this month. In order to thoroughly understand and prevent this, the Yellow River's ice run should be inspected and studied. It is reported that the commission has investigated the ice run conditions and losses in each section of Shaanxi, Henan, Hebei, and Shandong provinces over the past ten years, and has compiled detailed statistics. In addition to formulating ice prevention and guidance measures, it has also sent several engineers to inspect the upstream and downstream areas. (1) Carefully examine the ice sealing conditions, ice layer thickness, and its extension and thawing conditions, and record the location in detail. (2) Investigate the size of ice blocks, ice run speed, and its拥遏 gathering conditions, and carefully examine the damage to dams and slopes. (3) Study the formation of the ice body, the specific gravity of the ice, the amount of sand mixed in the ice, and the reasons for拥遏. Special attention should be paid to places that are prone to拥遏, and the effectiveness of various ice prevention and guidance methods should be inspected. It is recently heard that the commission has appointed Deputy Engineer Hua Guanshi and Assistant Engineer Xu Ruiao to inspect the Shili Pu and Qinghe Town areas of Shandong respectively, and Assistant Engineer Feng Tongyou to inspect the Hukou Longmen area. They departed from Bian yesterday and rushed to various places to work. (17th)

Recent Bandit Suppression Intelligence from Northeastern Fujian Province 91

—Huangkeng District, Jianyang County, Has Been Recovered—

Fuzhou Correspondence: After the Red Bandits in northern Fujian were defeated by the national army, the counties that had been lost have been completely recovered. The large Red Bandit forces have indeed been eliminated, but sporadic bandits still appear in the border areas of Fujian and Zhejiang, including Zhenghe, Songxi, Pucheng, Chong'an, and the border areas of Longquan, Qingyuan, Jiangshan, and Qianshan counties, causing great disturbances. Recently, Liu Heding, the Pacification Commander of northern Fujian, dispatched troops to encircle and suppress them, contacted each other, and advanced at the same time. Therefore, in recent days, the bandit suppression battles on the Fujian border have been quite fierce. According to military news yesterday, the Zhang Brigade of Chong'an used artillery to bombard the bandit bunkers in the Sidou area the day before, and after three hours of fierce fighting, occupied the large bandit bunkers. The remaining bandits rolled down the mountains and fled. The Zhang Brigade continued to advance and successively occupied several large bandit bunkers northeast of Wudou. The bandits fled to Yangzhuang and resisted stubbornly. The Zhang Brigade pursued and encircled them with all its strength and recovered Yangzhuang. The bandits collapsed towards Da'an. Also, the Huangkeng District of Jianyang County, which is adjacent to Chong'an and Pucheng, was occupied by bandits for three years. It has also recently been recovered by the Zhou Zhisun Brigade. The fake teaching regiment and five or six hundred guerrillas fled to Chong'an Guangze. However, the area has been ravaged by bandits for a long time and is extremely dilapidated. The Jianyang County Government telegraphed the province yesterday requesting that special commissioners be sent to provide relief and handle the aftermath as soon as possible. As for the eastern Fujian area, after Wang Jingjiu, the Garrison Commander of eastern Fujian, dispatched troops to encircle and suppress the bandit forces in Lianjiang and Luoyuan counties near the province, most of them have been eliminated, and only a few hundred people remain as small groups of sporadic bandits. Currently, in addition to deploying some troops to various districts to cooperate with local militias to search for sporadic bandits, another part of the troops is assisting the villagers in building roads to facilitate transportation. However, in the counties of Fu'an, Ningde, and Shouting, which are farther away from the province, Feng Pintai, the commander of the fake independent division, still commands Fan Tiemin, Ren Tiefeng, Ma Liefeng, and Xu Aman to appear and plunder. After consultation, Xiao Qian, the commander of the New Tenth Division, and Xu Hu, the administrative commissioner of the Second District, decided to advance separately and assign local security groups to intercept them, so as to eliminate the remaining bandits in a short period of time. (January 19)

This Year's Construction Plan for Fujian Province 92

—Stipulating Three Items: Water Conservancy, Agriculture and Forestry, and Highways—

Fuzhou Correspondence: The Fujian Provincial Government, now that the Red Bandits have been quelled and order is gradually stabilizing, has decided to undertake local construction starting in the 24th year [of the Republic, i.e., 1935], to seek the revitalization of society. However, due to financial difficulties, it has specially petitioned the Central Government to approve the issuance of construction bonds worth three million yuan for the purpose of handling agriculture, forestry, water conservancy, and highways. These bonds are guaranteed by the revenue from the provincial slaughter tax, with an annual interest rate of 7%, to be repaid in eight years. The principle has now been approved by the Executive Yuan, and issuance can begin once the Legislative Yuan passes it. As for the construction plan, it was decided by the Provincial Government Committee meeting to: (1) Establish a Provincial Water Conservancy General Engineering Office, abolishing the existing Min River Engineering Committee and the Changle Irrigation Engineering Office, and merging them into the new office to handle the planning and implementation of water conservancy projects throughout the province. The monthly expenses will be approximately 2,000 yuan. In addition to fully allocating the original expenses of the Min River Engineering Committee, which amounted to over 1,000 yuan, the Provincial Government will provide an additional 500 yuan per month. It is expected that the office can be established around February 1st, under the jurisdiction of the Construction Department. It is internally decided that Mr. Li will be the director. As the irrigation of farmland in Fujian Province relies entirely on natural rainfall and rivers, and suffers significant losses due to droughts, the office will prioritize the interests of farmland irrigation after its establishment. (2) Prepare for the establishment of a General Agriculture and Forestry Improvement Farm, and establish branch farms and nurseries in stages. The work plan of the farm is to improve agriculture and promote forestry. It is planned to establish agriculture farms in Changle, Nan'an, and Zhangpu counties, a forestry farm in Nanping, nurseries in Minhou and Putian counties, an insect research institute in Fuzhou, a livestock experiment farm, a Yongding tobacco improvement farm, a Fu'an tea improvement farm, a fertilizer management office, a Longxi sugarcane seedling farm, livestock farms in Jinjiang and Anxi counties, and rainfall measuring stations in fifteen counties including Minhou, Changle, Liancheng, Jiangle, Zhao'an, Wuping, Jianyang, Pucheng, Datian, Pingnan, Pingtan, Minqing, Hui'an, Fuzhou, and Longyan, as well as meteorological observatories in six locations: Fuzhou, Xiamen, Sandu, Tingzhou, Yanping, and Pucheng, to lay the foundation for improving agriculture and water conservancy. (3) The total length of the highway lines in Fujian Province is over 1,200 kilometers. The Construction Department completed the construction of over 400 kilometers last year. This year, it plans to construct three main lines: from Jianning through Ninghua and Changting to Ruijin, from Shaxian through Yong'an and Liancheng to Changting, and from Shaxian through Qingliu and Ninghua to Shicheng, connecting the hinterlands of the four provinces of Fujian, Guangdong, Jiangxi, and Zhejiang. The earthwork will be undertaken by road construction teams organized by the garrisons in the counties along the lines, and the stonework will be undertaken by the Construction Department's engineering team. The expenses will be shared equally between the central and local governments. Yesterday, the Construction Department dispatched Chief Engineer Chen Yusheng, Engineers Chen Weifan, Qian Naiqing, and Xiong Shiping, leading surveying teams to Shaxian, Jianning, and Changting to survey the routes in order to start construction. It is also borrowing 800,000 yuan from the Central Bank, using the Central Government's contribution as collateral, to be repaid in two years, for the construction costs. A portion has already been allocated yesterday. (January 16th)

Jiangsu Province Promotes Rural Sideline Occupations in Jiangbei 93

Zhenjiang News: In recent years, the rural economy in Jiangbei has become increasingly difficult. Chairman Chen of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, in view of this, proposed at the Provincial Government meeting on February 16th of last year to organize a Jiangsu Provincial Committee for Promoting Rural Sideline Occupations in Jiangbei, in order to alleviate the rural economy and stabilize the livelihoods of farmers in Jiangbei. The proposal was approved after discussion. Subsequently, the Provincial Government appointed design committee members, and the Construction Department convened the first meeting on March 2nd. At the same time, it ordered all counties to investigate suitable types of sideline occupations within their borders. The design committee compiled a plan for promoting rural sideline occupations in Jiangbei and various program rules, which were submitted to the Provincial Government meeting for approval and ordered the Jiangbei counties to comply. The promotion steps are divided into five categories: investigation, publicity, personnel training, research and discussion, and practical promotion. The promotion scope is divided into five categories: planting, animal husbandry, handicrafts, forestry, and fisheries. Each county will promote them separately according to their suitability. After receiving the orders, the counties were able to earnestly comply. Among them, the most popular were chrysanthemum and daylily in the planting category, chicken, pig, and bee in the animal husbandry category, weaving, wickerwork, and woolen shoes in the handicraft category, afforestation in the forestry category, and fishing in the fisheries category. The organization of various cooperatives and the establishment of sideline training classes were even more widespread. The promotion situation in each county is described below:

Nantong: (1) Advocate beekeeping. San Tou Xu has abundant honey sources and has been developed as a beekeeping area for demonstration. (2) Promote Langshan chickens. The Langshan Jiu Jin Wang chickens will be widely bred and sold at low prices. (3) Establish a native cloth production and sales cooperative. Native cloth produced in various places will be promoted and sold by the cooperative, and a native cloth inspection station will be established to improve the quality of native cloth. (4) Establish a straw hat braiding training class to teach farmers the technology of braiding straw hats. (5) Organize fish farming cooperatives, silkworm cocoon production and sales cooperatives, and improve pig farming.

Gaoyou: (1) Establish an autumn cocoon production and sales cooperative to facilitate public silkworm breeding and silk reeling. (2) Improve pig breeds. Purchase Berkshire pig breeds to cross with local pigs. (3) Organize fish farming cooperatives. Use abandoned water surfaces for fish farming. (4) Establish sideline technical training schools. The Public Education Center and Farmers' Education Center will be responsible for handling them separately, teaching farmers the technology of braiding straw hats and weaving lace.

Baoying: (1) Improve pig and chicken breeding. Purchase Berkshire pigs and Leghorn chickens for improvement. (2) Organize pig farming cooperatives to reduce production costs. (3) Establish sideline training classes to recruit farmers' children and teach them pig and chicken farming techniques. (4) Advocate special crops. Engage in the cultivation of chrysanthemum and daylily.

Huai'an: (1) Promote superior pig and chicken breeds. Use Berkshire pigs and Leghorn chickens to improve the original breeds. (2) Organize various production cooperatives. Fish farming and chicken farming cooperatives have now been established. (3) Use wasteland and barren shores to create forests and plant willows, etc.

Taixian: (1) Advocate braiding straw hats. The county has a lot of grass production, which is very suitable for promoting straw hat braiding among the people. (2) Refine small mill sesame oil. The county's small mill sesame oil is quite famous and has started to improve its quality and decoration. (3) Handle chicken, pig, bee, and fish farming cooperatives. (4) Prepare to establish training classes for sideline personnel.

Taixing: (1) Advocate special crops. The agricultural extension station first engaged in the demonstration cultivation of chrysanthemum and daylily and distributed them to farmers at low prices for trial planting to promote them. (2) Organize pig transport and sales and fish farming cooperatives. The county produces a lot of pigs. In order to facilitate transportation and sales, organize cooperatives. Also, use the water surface to organize fish farming cooperatives and engage in fish farming.

Rugao: (1) Prepare to establish paper mills. The county is planning to establish four paper mills to utilize rice straw, and is actively proceeding with them. (2) Use wasteland and barren mounds for afforestation. Afforest all the wasteland in the county as much as possible. (3) Advocate the cultivation of chrysanthemum. (4) Establish a civilian loan office. (5) Advocate chicken, pig, and bee farming.

Qidong: (1) Order all schools to use rural sideline teaching materials. (2) Organize fish farming cooperatives and distribute fish fry to nearby fishermen. (3) Establish a sock weaving training class. (4) Prepare to establish a civilian loan office and a farmers' bank agency.

Dongtai: (1) Improve chicken and pig breeding. Purchase Berkshire pigs and Leghorn chickens for improving the original breeds. (2) Establish a fishery training class to teach fishermen in the coastal area new fishing techniques. (3) Organize pig farming and other production and sales cooperatives. (4) Advocate the cultivation of special crops such as chrysanthemum and daylily.

Fengxian: (1) Advocate the manufacture of earth nitrate. The county produces a lot of earth nitrate, which is the main sideline occupation of the people. (2) Establish a wickerwork weaving training class. Hire wickerwork technicians to teach people how to weave. (3) Improve the weaving of woolen shoes and reed mats. (4) Improve fruits. Xiaoxian: (1) Advocate the brewing of grape wine. The county is rich in grapes. Technicians have now been hired to start brewing grape wine. (2) Advocate machine oil extraction and cotton ginning. This matter is in progress. (3) Improve fruits. The county is rich in peaches, plums, pears, pomegranates, and other fruits.

Pixian: (1) Organize transport and sales cooperatives. The county's woolen shoes and cattail leaf fans have always been famous. In order to facilitate transportation and sales, organize cooperatives. (2) Establish sideline training classes. (3) Advocate pig and chicken farming.

Jiangdu: (1) Improve pig breeding. There are many pig farmers in the second and seventh districts of the county. Use Berkshire pigs to cross with local pigs for breeding. (2) Advocate chicken and duck farming. (3) Organize fish farming cooperatives.

Xinghua: (1) Plant willows and reeds. The terrain in the 22nd district of the county is low-lying, which is suitable for planting willows and reeds. (2) Improve pig and chicken farming. (3) Organize fish farming and reed mat weaving production and sales cooperatives.

Yancheng: (1) Advocate the manufacture of lime from clam shells. The clam shells produced in the coastal area can be ground into fine powder to replace lime. It is now being actively promoted. (2) Establish a sideline demonstration area. It will be held in Yongxie Township, the eighth district of the county. (3) Establish sideline training classes for weaving towels and socks.

Peixian: (1) Promote seedlings. The Agricultural Extension Station is responsible. (2) Handle sideline technical training classes. The Farmers' Education Center is responsible.

Suqian: (1) Train sideline people. First set up a wickerwork weaving training class. (2) Promote daylily. The county cultivates a lot of this vegetable, and the profit is also high. It is now being promoted even more. (3) Hold agricultural product exhibitions.

Haimen: (1) Organize fish farming cooperatives. Use the abandoned water surface along the river to engage in aquaculture. (2) Advocate chicken and pig farming. (3) Advocate beekeeping.

Chongming: (1) Advocate the cultivation of yellow sprouts. The yellow sprouts produced in the county are of good quality and are now being promoted even more. (2) Improve native cloth. The native cloth produced in the county sells well in the Haizhou area. (3) Organize fish farming cooperatives.

Yizheng: (1) Improve the technology of knitting nets, weaving reed mats, and twisting palm ropes. The county produces a lot of fishing nets, reed mats, and palm ropes. Now, we are trying to improve them. (2) Advocate chicken, pig, and fish farming.

Funing: (1) Use wasteland for afforestation. Plant willows in gaps. (2) Organize cotton production and sales cooperatives.

Jingjiang: (1) Use abandoned water surfaces for fish farming. (2) Organize cooperatives.

Yangzhong: (1) Organize bamboo and wood transport and sales cooperatives. The county produces a lot of bamboo and wood. In order to facilitate transportation and sales, organize bamboo and wood transport and sales cooperatives. (2) Advocate fish farming. Purchase fish fry and distribute them to farmers for breeding. (3) Use wasteland to plant mulberry trees and afforest.

Siyang: (1) Advocate the planting of daylily and fruit trees. (2) Improve chicken and pig farming. (3) Investigate paper making and charcoal burning industries. (4) Organize various transport and sales cooperatives.

Huaiyin: (1) Establish training classes for weaving cloth and weaving wickerwork. (2) Improve chicken and pig farming.

Ganyu: (1) Set up sideline training classes. (2) Improve chicken farming and fishing.

Dangshan: (1) Advocate weaving cloth and weaving wickerwork. (2) Improve Dangshan pears.

Weining: (1) Establish sideline training classes. (2) Organize production cooperatives.

Shuyang: (1) Improve pig farming. (2) Advocate small handicrafts.

Looking at the situation of promoting rural sideline occupations in various counties in Jiangbei, fish farming, chicken farming, and pig farming are more common in the areas along the river, followed by weaving cloth, knitting nets, and cultivating special crops. In the Huaiyang area, chicken farming, fish farming, and pig farming are more common, followed by straw hat braiding and beekeeping. In the Xuhai area, chicken farming, oil pressing, and wine brewing are more common. In the counties under Xuzhou, fruit trees are especially important. As for the establishment of sideline cooperatives and sideline training classes, it is quite common. This is the general situation of promoting rural sideline occupations in Jiangbei. Among them, the grape wine in Xiaoxian, the cloth production and sales cooperative in Nantong, and the large-scale beekeeping industry in Rugao have achieved particularly remarkable results. In order to actively promote rural sideline occupations in various counties in Jiangbei, the Construction Department is still urging all counties to earnestly handle them. If given time, the future development of rural sideline occupations in Jiangbei can be predicted.

Changshu

Tenant Farmers Go on Hunger Strike to Resist Military Training 95

Since the establishment of the rent collection office in the county, dozens of landlords have requested the arrest of tenant farmers every day. Recently, as the end of the lunar year is approaching, there has been an even greater influx of requests for arrest. Since February, the number of people arrested and sent to the detention center has reached more than 280, and will soon exceed this number. In order to increase the effectiveness of rent collection, the county government ordered the security team to take the detained tenant farmers to the stadium every day for military training, falsely claiming that they would be sent to the front line when necessary. Recently, the tenant farmers learned of this and, after training the day before yesterday, agreed not to eat lunch. The warden was quite shocked and reported it to the county magistrate. Therefore, the detained tenant farmers are no longer subjected to military training, but are instead assigned to labor service.

Traffickers in Humans Arrested and Sent to Court for Trial 96

On the 15th of this month, the Wuxi County Public Security Bureau's Supervision Division cracked down on the Southeast Human Trafficking Headquarters in Xiang'an Lane on the road. The main criminals, Ma Zishan and other men and women, ten in total, were arrested on the spot. Because the case still had developments, it was not until yesterday that the one thousand criminals were transferred to the local branch court for trial. Wine and Sauce Industry Appeals for Exemption from Duplicate Tax 97

The wine and sauce shops in this county, such as Yifeng, Chen Jinfeng, Hongtai, and Tongren, believe that since they have already paid the tobacco and alcohol license tax, the Wuxi District Xishi Tax Bureau under the Yingxi Tax Bureau is not complying with the exemption regulations of the Business Tax Law, and is still mixing the tobacco and alcohol items that have already been licensed with other sundries sold at the same time, and repeatedly collecting business tax together, which increases the additional burden on merchants and is an illegal overcharge that harms merchants and the people. Therefore, yesterday they jointly sent a letter to the trade association, requesting that the county chamber of commerce be immediately requested to forward a letter to the Business Tax Bureau to remove the tobacco and alcohol items and exempt them from tax in order to comply with the law.

Changzhou

Wujin and Yixing Counties Jointly Investigate the Abandoned Corpse by the Lake 98

In Caoshu Town, the eighth district of Wujin County, a bizarre murder case was rumored to have occurred last month. It was said that Zhou Zhongsheng, the town mayor and head of the self-defense regiment, had an affair with the daughter of a Mr. Sun, the owner of Rencun Sauce Garden. Recently, the woman had an affair with a clerk in the shop. Zhou Zhongsheng hated it to the core. One day, the clerk went on a secret rendezvous, which Zhou found out about. He immediately sent militiamen to surround them. The clerk dashed out, was shot and wounded, and stabbed to death with a bayonet. Afterwards, the body was abandoned in Taihu Lake to cover up the traces. Newspapers in Wuxi and Wujin counties competed to publish the story. Yang Kongxi, the chief prosecutor of the Wujin County Court, summoned Zhou Zhongsheng and others for interrogation once, but ordered them to return home because there was no corroborating evidence. Chief Prosecutor Yang believed that the case was important. He secretly went to investigate on the 17th of this month. On the 18th, the court suddenly received a telegram from the Yixing County Government, saying that a male corpse with gunshot wounds had been found in Chenshu Village, Fenshuidun, by Taihu Lake. It was feared that it was related to the Caoshu Bridge murder case, and they requested that personnel be sent to conduct a joint investigation. The court immediately dispatched investigator Shen Shaochun to Caoshu Bridge to report to Chief Prosecutor Yang, and the Yixing trial officer Qiu Hongzao had also arrived. They went to the lake together on the morning of the 19th to conduct a joint investigation. It was determined that the corpse was about 30 years old, had two gold teeth in its mouth, had a gunshot wound on its waist, three knife wounds, and multiple overlapping knife wounds on its lower abdomen. It was determined that the victim had been shot and then stabbed to death with overlapping knife wounds before his death. After the investigation, the village head was ordered to provide a coffin for burial and report it to the Yixing County Government. Trial Officer Qiu of Yixing left for Yixing. Chief Prosecutor Yang believed that the case seemed to be closely related to the suspected adultery case, so he returned to Caoshu Bridge. At the district office, he summoned Zhou Zhongsheng, Lu Zhengjun, a shareholder of the sauce garden, Han Chuanbao, a boatman, Zhou Fulin, a night watchman, and Qiu Changsheng, a self-defense regiment instructor, for interrogation, believing that they were highly suspected. He ordered them to be released on bail separately and ordered them to come to the court on the 23rd to await interrogation.

Jiashan

Two Villages Fight Over Temple Property 99

Yongfu Nunnery, an ancient temple in Beichi Village, Dingzha Town, was built during the Chongzhen period of the late Ming Dynasty. It is surrounded by pine and cypress trees and has abundant temple property. In the early years of the Republic, Li Dexiang came forward and introduced the monk Songting from Shujia Village to preside over the nunnery and set up a rural private school. Unexpectedly, Songting ignored the nunnery affairs and even sold ancient trees and used the proceeds for personal purposes. Recently, Shen Baode from the village, in order to preserve the ancient relics, specially invited donors and raised funds for renovation. When Songting received the news, he sneaked into the nunnery and erected a plaque, intending to show that he had repaired it. The villagers found out about this and questioned the monk. Songting became angry out of shame and colluded with Chen Yuqi, the village head of Beichi Village, to gather more than 50 people from Dongchi Village, each holding iron tools, and swarm to force Sun Bingxiang, a donor from Dongchi, to sign a statement acknowledging that the Yongfu Nunnery property would be managed by him in the future and that Songting would still be the abbot. Sun refused, stating that the nunnery was built by Beichi Village and there was a monument to prove it. Chen then ordered them to be beaten. The gengchu hoes came down at the same time and the order was in chaos. Chen Linsheng, Li Yulai, Li Dianxin, and others were injured on the spot. The Dingzha Public Security Bureau received the news and sent police to suppress it overnight.

Nantong

Nantong District徵工 Dredges Rivers 100

All the rivers, big and small, in the counties under the Nantong District have been approved by the Administrative Inspector Commissioner's Office and the Construction Department to send Guiding Engineer Gao Suokan to supervise the counties to conscript laborers to dredge and manage them. Rugao and Jingjiang have been completed. There are some disputes in Tonghai and other counties. The Commissioner's Office has convened a meeting to decide that Haimen and Nantong are related to the river and that Nantong will be responsible for providing labor assistance. The maximum limit is one-quarter of the total number, which will start next month.

Hangzhou

A Major Fire in Xingzhong Lane Yesterday Morning 101

At 12:00 p.m. on the 19th, a fire suddenly broke out in Qian Daheng Silk Shop at No. 29, Xingzhong Lane, Hangzhou City, due to a short circuit. The fire was quite fierce. Lu Weiquan, the owner of the shop, and his family members and partners were all awakened from their sleep and rushed out of the door to jump from the building to escape. Fire brigades and foreign volunteers rushed to the scene to put out the fire. It was not extinguished until 1:20 a.m. today (20th). It is estimated that three halls and the accumulated goods were burned, worth about 30,000 yuan. Lu's mother-in-law, Ye Wang, was injured in both legs from jumping from the building and was sent to the hospital for treatment. Lu's wife, Wang, and her sister, Yuexian, and the maidservant were slightly injured and there was no major problem. In addition, Xu Liusan's family at No. 1, Jixiang Temple, west of Gongbu Bridge, caught fire due to a kerosene lamp falling over. It was extinguished after being watered down. Nine thatched houses were burned, and the loss was limited.

Young Girls and Boys Reported Missing 102

Ai Yun, the 16-year-old daughter of Zhu Dequan, a Shaoxing native at No. 6, Sanbao, Hushu, has been betrothed to someone. The day before yesterday morning, due to family matters, Zhu reprimanded her slightly. Unexpectedly, the girl ran away in a fit of anger. Her mother, feeling sorry for her daughter, searched everywhere and was run over by a car and injured her foot. Zhu is also bedridden, which is quite pitiful. In addition, Tu Gen, the eight-year-old son of Wang Sanbao at No. 5, Sanguan Lane, Zhong'an Bridge, who is studying at a nearby elementary school, suddenly went missing the day before yesterday afternoon. The police station has been notified to investigate.

Jiaxing

A Vendetta Murder Case Occurred on Youguang Bridge 103

Li Baokui, a foreign overseas Chinese citizen, about 50 years old, who lived about two li from Youguang Bridge, sixth district of Jiaxing, used to be a water police detective. During his tenure, he had repeatedly solved major cases. He is now retired and living at home, making a living by farming, and has hired a long-term worker, Yu Zaogui, to help with farming. Unexpectedly, at 8:00 p.m. on the 17th, Li had already fallen asleep when he suddenly heard a urgent knock on the door. When Li put on his clothes and opened the door, he was shot. Yu heard the gunshot and knew that something was wrong, but he dared not go out to see. After a while, there was no sound. He went to Li's house to see that Li had been shot several times and died. That night, Yu reported to the police station, which sent police to investigate. However, the bandits had already disappeared.

The Third Anniversary of "January 28th" is Approaching 105

Party Headquarters Preparing to Hold a Commemorative Meeting

The third anniversary of "January 28th" is approaching. The Propaganda Section of the headquarters is actively preparing for the commemorative methods and meeting staff. Military and police authorities, fearing that reactionary elements will take the opportunity to cause trouble, will announce joint precautions to avoid accidents.

The Reputation of National Products is Increasing Daily 107

South African Merchant Comes to China to Negotiate Samples

The Production and Sales Company Has Handled More Than Ten Cases on Behalf

Guowen News Agency reports: In recent years, the domestic goods market has spared no effort in developing the domestic goods industry. New products are emerging like bamboo shoots after the rain. The people's belief in using domestic goods has become increasingly strong, and the number of users is gradually increasing. Since the Chicago Exposition in the United States, the activities of Chinese national products in the international arena have also become more flexible. British Chamber of Commerce Announces Sharp Decline in Sino-British Trade 108

Sales of Yarn and Cloth Are Shrinking Daily

Japanese Competition is Still Fierce

East China News Agency reports: The Manchester Chamber of Commerce in Shanghai issued its annual report on British trade with China yesterday, stating that China has become quieter, but trade activities have declined. It also stated that the decline in China's purchasing power is the main reason for the rapid decline in the Lancashire textile trade. For the past ten years, China has been a customer for British cotton yarn and cotton cloth, but recently, the sales of British yarn and cloth in China have been shrinking daily. In the first eleven months of 1934, the total export volume to China was only 11% of that in the same period of 1932. The way to improve the situation is to wait until China can sell its products at better prices domestically or until the demand for its products increases. Japanese competition is still fierce, mainly because of its proximity to China and convenient transportation. However, Japan's export trade is also gradually declining. It also stated that the frequent changes in Chinese tariffs make buyers cautious, which reduces trade and leads to a shortage of tax revenue. The current high tax rate is enough to encourage large-scale smuggling, etc.

French Colony to Increase Tea Tax 109

Chinese Tea Exports to France Will Come to a Standstill

Tea Merchants Petition the Government to Negotiate

Last year, China's tea exports made considerable progress, especially in black tea, in addition to green tea. The same was true for exports to France. Due to the French government's increase in tea taxes in April last year, a total of 3,576 metric tons were exported to France in the first eleven months, a decrease of 44% compared to 6,379 metric tons in the same period of the 22nd year of the Republic (1933), a particularly severe decline. Black tea amounted to 9,691 metric tons, an increase of more than one and a half times compared to 3,821 metric tons in the same period of the 22nd year of the Republic (1933). Without tax restrictions, the increase rate would have been even higher. According to Chen Yizhou, a representative of the foreign tea trade association, the French colony of Algeria sells about 50,000 boxes of high-quality green tea such as Wuyuan Yinguang Zhenmei every year (about 65 catties per box). The tax collection method in the 23rd year of the Republic (1934) was about 8 jiao per catty. It is now planned to double the tax collection from January of this year. Therefore, tea merchants are greatly panicked. They previously sent a telegram to the Ministry of Industry and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, requesting them to instruct the Chinese ambassador to France to negotiate with the French authorities to avoid increasing taxes. It is rumored that the French government plans to postpone the implementation for 45 days, until February 15th, but the new tea must be shipped to Shanghai for export between May and June. Even if the postponement is true, it will be of no avail. It is understood that the purpose of the French tax increase is to increase revenue. However, if this is implemented, our exports to Algeria will likely stop completely. In reality, the French may not benefit much, while our losses will be very heavy. The reason is that Chinese green tea has always relied on Morocco and Algeria as its final destination. In the midst of declining exports last year, there was an increase in exports to Algeria, with a total of 20,152 metric tons in the first eleven months, valued at 2,260,292 yuan, an increase of 2,773 metric tons and 270,264 yuan. In the future, the result of the tax increase will undoubtedly be the loss of a major market for green tea, and Japan will have another opportunity to compete for sales. At a time when the domestic export industry is declining, the seriousness of this issue is worthy of attention. Some say that if the French tax increase is inevitable, China can also choose important French imports and increase taxes on them to counter it. The idea is good, and it may be an effective countermeasure, but we believe that the long-standing friendly relations and flourishing trade between China and France should not be reduced by a tariff war. All tea merchants in Shanghai are currently preparing to submit a petition, requesting the Ministry of Industry and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to instruct the Chinese ambassador to negotiate with France to avoid imposing heavy taxes.

The annual interest rate is 1%. At that time, the principal and interest will be fully repaid. Complete Shutdown As Usual When Closing Accounts

Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Petitions for the Formulation of a Common Civil Etiquette System 118

Etiquette is One of the Major Laws of the Country

Old Etiquette is Largely Incompatible with the Present

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce petitioned the Legislative Yuan yesterday, stating that it was petitioning for the matter. The Beijing Chamber of Commerce sent a letter requesting assistance in advocating for the Legislative Yuan to stipulate a common etiquette system for civilians in order to bring the people back on track. It was stated in the original case that the Republic of China has been established for twenty-three years, and only the rituals for audience and awarding medals have been established. The rituals for civil marriages, funerals, condolences, and meetings have not been stipulated, allowing people to do as they please, resulting in strange situations and harming the national system. After verifying the points raised in the petition, it was found that they were in line with the actual situation. In the past, the state's system of rites and music was always established after governance was successful. In recent years, the situation has been turbulent, and the major policies of the country are awaiting attention, so the rituals have not been amended. Even the general public always considers this matter to be delayed. However, as a result of the reform of the national system, the old etiquette is largely incompatible with the present. This is different from the situation at the turn of dynasties, where the etiquette system of the previous dynasty can be inherited. If everything is modeled after Europe and the United States, it will not only be incompatible with the national conditions but will also lead to conflicts and a loss of the national independence and self-respect. Moreover, etiquette is one of the major laws of the country. It falls under the jurisdiction of your esteemed Yuan and is the responsibility of a dedicated department. It does not mean that the unfinished military affairs will prevent its deliberate discussion. The matter can be carried out in parallel without any conflict. It is different from the past system of rites and music, which must be established after the situation is settled and the task is accomplished. It is reasonable to submit the true situation to your esteemed Yuan for review, and it would be a public convenience if you would immediately refer to and amend it. Respectfully submitted.

Page 11

Ministry of Communications Disapproves Extension of the Deadline for Closing Private Postal Agencies, to Be Reorganized into Forwarding Agencies 128

Draft Plan Drawn Up Seeking Opinions from the Industry

Livelihood Relief Difficulties for Tens of Thousands of Employees

Dagong News Agency reports that since January 1st of this year, the Postal Administration officially abolished the weighing regulations and punished private delivery of letters, the business of private postal agencies in Shanghai has been completely suspended. The national postal merchants previously petitioned the central government to revoke the ban order, but the Ministry of Communications has issued an order disapproving it. Therefore, local postal agencies plan to reorganize into forwarding agencies to handle parcel and silver ocean business. The details are as follows.

Ministry of Communications Issues Order Disapproving 129

In December of last year, the National Federation of Private Postal Agencies sent seven chief representatives, including Wu Jinyun and Yin Yuantong, to Beijing to petition the National Government, the Fifth Plenary Session, the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Communications, the Ministry of Industry, and other agencies, requesting the revocation of the order to end the business of private postal agencies. The Ministry of Communications formally issued an order to the delegation, stating that there was no need to discuss the request to revoke the order or extend the deadline. However, in consideration of the livelihood of merchants and employees, silver ocean parcels, etc., that are not associated with private postal services may still be delivered as usual.

Business Completely Suspended 130

The original deadline for the closure of private postal agencies was the end of December of last year, and all business was to be suspended. Because postal merchants wanted to maintain their livelihood, they continued to operate until they received a reply from the central government. The Shanghai Post Office, in order to implement the orders of the superiors, sent personnel to inspect the districts and arrested and detained postal workers and seized letters from Baoshun on Jiujiang Road and Quanchang on Xian Gua Street. Although the private postal agencies set up stations for delivery, senders, in order to avoid losses, sent all letters, silver oceans, and parcels through the post office. Therefore, since January 5th of this year, the business of various private postal agencies in Shanghai has been completely suspended. Even the number of silver ocean parcels sent to Ningbo, Wenzhou, and the interior is very small. Thousands of employees are staying in the agency, and the situation is very pitiful.

Plan to Establish a Forwarding Agency 131

Since the Ministry of Communications issued an order disapproving the extension and business has been suspended, the income of private postal agencies in Shanghai is very small, while the food and accommodation of employees still need to be provided, resulting in heavy losses. Now that the Ministry of Communications has approved the remittance of silver ocean parcels, the delegation of chief representatives of the National Federation of Private Postal Agencies discussed the final solution and planned to reorganize the existing private postal agencies into forwarding agencies. This matter is of great importance and requires a large amount of funding. It has been notified to fellow industries in various places to solicit opinions before a decision can be made.

Difficulties in Employee Relief 132

After receiving the order from the Executive Yuan, the Shanghai Municipal Government repeatedly ordered the Social Affairs Bureau and the Public Security Bureau to persuade the postal merchants to close their businesses. The Public Security Bureau sent personnel to investigate the business and number of employees of the private postal agencies in detail and discussed solutions. A Dagong News Agency reporter inquired at the private postal agency association about the employee relief issue. The person in charge replied that if the reorganization of the forwarding agency is successful and it specializes in remitting silver ocean parcels, the number of employees will naturally be reduced. If the reorganization cannot be achieved, they will be unemployed. The livelihood of tens of thousands of people is very serious, and they hope that the central government will care about the people's livelihood and provide them with proper resettlement. They also plan to gather postal merchants from all over the country to petition the central government again.

Li Du and Others Initiate the Establishment of a Northeast Shanghai Native Place Association 133

Chongming Association in Shanghai Launches Chongqi Merger Movement 135

Initiate the Organization of a Committee to Promote the Merger

Elder Wang Qingmu Bitterly Speaks of the Evils of Division

Shanghai News reports: Chongming is located at the mouth of the river, with a dangerous terrain and a vital strategic position. In the past, it was an important naval town and the gateway to the Yangtze River. Originally, the inner and outer sandbars were combined into one county, and they lived in peace. However, since the Republic of China, a few people from the outer sandbar and 海门 (Haimen) people living in the outer sandbar, such as 施滋培 (Shi Zipei), have repeatedly requested division. After the sixteenth year, 施 (Shi) and others took advantage of the fact that the National Revolutionary Army had just pacified the Yangtze River, and actively engaged in the division movement in various ways. In February of the seventeenth year, the formal division was established. As a result, government expenses increased sharply, land taxes soared, and the people suffered deeply. Although the Chongming people sent telegrams and letters to express their opposition, the national and provincial governments were misled by preconceived notions and did not consult them. In recent years, the rural economy has become increasingly collapsed. The county has been affected by the division, water conservancy has been neglected, and droughts and floods have caused disasters. The people's livelihood is on the verge of collapse, and education fees are in arrears for more than ten months. There is also no ability to repair the bank protection and embankment projects. Therefore, the people of the county feel that they cannot survive unless they request a merger. There have been repeated petitions, and the fellow villagers of the two counties of Chongqi, who live in Beijing, 镇江 (Zhenjiang), 平 (Ping), and Shanghai, have also sent letters and telegrams to the government, requesting a merger. The Shanghai News reporter has specially investigated the situation from all parties for this matter and recorded it as follows:

Expand the Merger Movement 136

The Chongming Association in Shanghai was originally organized by 童行白 (Tong Xingbai), 杨震中 (Yang Zhenzhong), 陈东白 (Chen Dongbai), 施翀鹏 (Shi Chongpeng), and others from the county. It has now been formally established. When the first board of directors meeting was held, the proposal for promoting the merger of Chongqi submitted by the general meeting was discussed. It was unanimously decided to unite various groups in the native county and fellow villagers' groups in various places to initiate the organization of a committee to promote the merger of Chongqi. 理事 (Li Shi) 施翀鹏 (Shi Chongpeng) was entrusted to draft the preamble, and it was decided to hold a provisional board of directors meeting on the 22nd of this month to discuss the matter specifically. After the preamble is approved, the committee will be organized in conjunction with all parties to actively promote the merger in order to achieve the goal of merger.

Elder Wang Qingmu Speaks 137

Yesterday, the reporter interviewed the county elder, the former Director of the Taihu Water Conservancy Bureau, and the current member of the National Government's Huai River Guidance Committee, Wang Qingmu. According to him, the discussion of the division of Chongqi began in the early years of the Republic of China. 施滋培 (Shi Zipei), a 海门 (Haimen) person living in the outer sandbar, repeatedly requested the establishment of a separate county, but the provincial government did not allow it. Eight years later, the representatives from the inner and outer sandbars negotiated the plan at the 海道尹 (Haidaoyin) Public Office in Shanghai, such as adding administrative members, judicial reviewers, and separate grain collection offices to the outer sandbar. Everything that could facilitate the outer sandbar was taken care of, and the people of the outer sandbar lived in peace for a long time. It was suddenly divided in the seventeenth year. To explain the reason, it is extremely simple. To put it briefly, the inner and outer sandbars of Chongming can be compared to mother and son. The son never wanted to separate from his mother, establish a separate household, increase expenses, and cause more waste. However, several servants of the son seized the son and separated from the mother. After the separation, the mother and son were separated, and several servants either occupied the accounting room or held the silver box, and the owner could not interfere. The mother's property deposited with the son was confiscated. As a result, mother and son both felt pain and groaned endlessly. 清穆 (Qingmu) (self-proclaimed) is a servant on the mother's side and has no responsibility for management. He only hopes that the head of the family is upright, warns the servants, and allows the mother and son to reunite.

The Evils of Division Over the Years 138

Wang also spoke about the economic situation before and after the division, the gap between the high and low, and the difficulty of the people's power. Before the division, the inner and outer sandbars of Quan Chongming bore 22,000 taels of busy silver. After the division, the outer sandbar became Qidong, and the land area was reduced by most, while the inner sandbar still bore the entire amount. The outer sandbar separately levied more than 26,000 taels of busy silver, and the burden of provincial expenses more than doubled. If the local expenses are concerned, before the division, the budget for the 14th year of the Republic of China for the inner and outer sandbars of Chongming was 88,354 yuan in total for both regular and temporary items. After the division, the budget for Qidong in the 22nd year of the Republic of China was 449,875 yuan in total for both regular and temporary items. The budget for Chongming was 489,087 yuan in total for both regular and temporary items. The two totaled 938,963 yuan, an increase of nearly twelve times. It is difficult for the poor people of Chongqi to bear more than double the provincial expenses and twelve times the local expenses. It is like a thin sheep being burdened with ten catties, and now it is suddenly burdened with one hundred and twenty or thirty catties. Is it not on the verge of death? However, with such a large amount of provincial expenses used as county administrative expenses, it is still considered insufficient, and a surcharge of five cents is added to each tael of busy silver. With such a large amount of local expenses allocated to the two counties' internal affairs, charity, industry, finance, administration, social affairs, and cultural undertakings, there are times when it is not enough. The people's wealth has been exhausted, and the government's economy is still in trouble. To remedy this situation, the only way is to quickly merge, save expenses, reduce the burden, and the benefits will be immediately realized. Recently, I heard that the provincial government, taking into account the difficult situation of Chongqi, has submitted the merger issue to the financial, educational, and construction departments for deliberation and implementation. If it can be merged, then our 800,000 people will be able to see the light of day again and get rid of hidden pain.

Lawyer Liu Bin is Proposed for Disciplinary Action 148

Lawyer Liu Bin, a local, was previously arrested by the French Concession Patrol Bureau for collecting fees on behalf of others for obtaining stall licenses for the Julai Da Road vegetable market from the French Public Works Bureau. He was sent to the Second Special Court and prosecuted for fraud. After trial, he was sentenced to eight months in prison and fined 200 yuan. Subsequently, after the Collegial Panel's trial, the sentence was changed to a fine of 800 yuan. After receiving the final judgment, Liu immediately paid the fine. In accordance with the instructions of the Judicial Administration Department No. 15307 of the previous year, only those who have been sentenced to imprisonment or detention should be suspended from practicing as lawyers. Now that the sentence has been changed to a fine, his lawyer qualifications should be restored. He sent a letter to the Shanghai Lawyers Association to forward it to the legal courts at all levels for approval to restore his lawyer duties. This has been reported in previous news. The Suspect in the Shooting of the Indian Police Officer Changes His Confession 151

Zhou Hongtian Ordered to be Returned to Custody Yesterday

Wang Jinsheng Handed Over to the Second Special Court

On the evening of December 9th last year, at 10:45 PM, Indian policeman No. 258 of the Yangshupu Patrol Bureau was shot and seriously injured while patrolling on Hejian Road. He was sent to the hospital for treatment but died. At that time, a gray felt copper pot hat and a cartridge case were left at the scene. Later, Chinese detective Su Yinggen received a report from an informant and, in cooperation with Chinese detective Liu Wenzao and detective Hua Shouqi, arrested the suspects, Zhou Hongtian and Wang Jinsheng, from Taizhou, on Aiduya Road, Xizang Road, and the Gongguan Malu Mofang Street in the French Concession. They were sent to the First Special District Court and blamed each other. The case was under investigation. The day before yesterday afternoon, Judge Wu Tingqi came to the Second Criminal Court for trial. Lawyer Li Zhishan of the Public Works Bureau stated that the handgun used to shoot the Indian police officer was made in China, specifically at the former Shanghai Arsenal, with the words "Shanghai" and the number 2740. On the 16th of the same month, the defendant Wang Jinsheng colluded with the already arrested thief Wang Jinfa by the French Concession Patrol Bureau to rob a resident at 263 Baer Road. The Second Special District Court has dispatched bailiffs to the court. The defendant Zhou Hongtian admitted at the patrol bureau that he and Wang Jinsheng went to Yangshupu to rob a property. He had a Shanghai brand handgun, but because Wang Jinsheng did not have a gun, he was afraid it would be difficult to achieve their goal. They saw a Japanese police officer No. 42 walking on the road and tried to seize his pistol but failed. They changed their plan and then shot the Indian police officer from behind. The officer was hit and fell. In panic, he abandoned his felt hat and fled to the French Concession where he was arrested. He presented his confession. He also stated that the handgun was seized by the French Concession Patrol Bureau when Wang Jinfa was arrested. A Westerner from the Public Patrol Bureau's handgun department examined the bullets inside and found that they were identical to the bullet removed from the Indian police officer's body and the cartridge case found at the scene. Enlarged photos were taken and submitted. He questioned Zhou Hongtian, who suddenly changed his confession, saying that what he said at the patrol bureau was not voluntary. In fact, the person who shot and injured the Indian police officer at the time was a man named Bao Gan who was at large. The remainder of his confession was evasive. Wang Jinsheng also changed his confession, claiming that at the time, Bao sent him to Yangshupu to visit a friend, and that Bao was the one who fired the shot at the Indian police officer. Although he knew Wang Jinfa, who was arrested in the French Concession, he did not go to rob the Baer Road property with him. Lawyer Li also stated that the Indian police officer, before his death in the hospital, said that there were only two murderers. Therefore, the confessions of the two defendants were false. According to the public notice submitted by Bailiff Liu, he requested that Wang Jinsheng be taken away to be interrogated together with Wang Jinfa and then returned. The court approved it. Lawyer Li also stated that, after the adjournment, the two defendants, accompanied by Chinese and Western detectives, went to the scene to demonstrate in detail how they shot the Indian police officer and fled. Judge Wu ordered that the case be adjourned to the 16th for further questioning. Zhou Hongtian was returned to custody, and Wang Jinsheng was taken away by the police from the Second Special Court for interrogation and then returned. Wang Jinfa must be brought forward for questioning when the time comes.

Fire on Xujiahui Road Last Night 153

San Zhi Silk Factory Loses Ten Thousand Yuan

The Zhenhua Silk Factory, located at No. 10 Jintong Village, Xujiahui Road, French Concession, and owned by Yu Nianfang, caught fire last night around 9:00 PM. The flames quickly spread, and the fire was raging. Before long, it spread to the adjacent Taijiu Silk Factory (owned by Wang Jiuxiang) at No. 9 and the Yufeng Heng Silk Factory (owned by Shi Jichang) at No. 8. County Smokers to be Weaned in Stages 154

The Shanghai County Anti-Smoking Committee has drafted measures for weaning smokers in the county in stages. It has been found that the county's anti-smoking center can accommodate a number of smokers. Excluding those under compulsion for investigation, it can accommodate 30 people, in two batches per month, which is 60 people. Based on a detailed estimate of the total number of smokers, they can be completely weaned within three years. The measures for phased smoking cessation implemented by the committee are based on the seniority of age, with the young being weaned first, and if the ages are the same, those with lighter smoking habits are weaned first. Those who should be weaned but cannot be weaned due to illness must be diagnosed and confirmed by a doctor at the county's anti-smoking center before they can be allowed to postpone the weaning. The committee will notify the smokers who should be weaned in stages to come to the center for weaning, starting from November of this year. Every half month, 30 people will be weaned in turn, starting with the youngest.

Mongolia Road Police Station Cracks Down on Counterfeit Money Offenders 155

At 7:40 PM the day before yesterday, Zhao Guanying, the police officer at the 16th post of the Tianbao Li Police Station, which belongs to the Mongolia Road Police Station in Zhabei, heard a commotion at the Ninganfang intersection on North Zhejiang Road while on duty. He immediately stepped forward to inquire. A fruit seller named Yuan Zichun claimed that he (referring to the other party) used a one-yuan counterfeit banknote from the Bank of China to buy two oranges from him, asking him to give change. He discovered that it was a counterfeit note, but he refused to exchange it back and even tried to beat him. While the police officer was questioning him, three more counterfeit notes of the same kind were suddenly found on the ground. A search of his body revealed ten one-yuan counterfeit banknotes and two ten-yuan counterfeit banknotes from the Bank of China in his crotch, as well as one five-yuan counterfeit banknote from the Central Bank and three ten-yuan counterfeit banknotes from the China and South Bank. The police officer Zhao knew that he was not a good person, so he immediately took him and the fruit seller Yuan Zichun to the station. After questioning by Inspector Li Yiqian, the suspect confessed that his name was Tian Hongchun, 43 years old, and he was from Ying County. He had been in Changzhou and had just come to Shanghai today (the day before yesterday). He admitted that the counterfeit banknotes were purchased from a Mr. Wang at No. 10 Chengmei Li, Fangbang Road, Nanshi. After hearing the confession, Inspector Li immediately escorted the suspect Tian to Nanshi with detective Sun Youzhi and others from the Mongolia Road Police Station. They went to No. 10 Chengmei Li, Fangbang Road, together with the Laobeimen Police Station, but Mr. Wang had already fled upon hearing the news. Only seven business cards of Tian Hongchun, a name stamp, and two photos were found and taken to the station. After further questioning, the prosecutor Yuan Zichun and the defendant Tian Hongchun, along with 69 yuan of counterfeit banknotes, were sent to the Zhabei branch of the Third Section of the Public Security Bureau yesterday morning. Yesterday was Sunday, so they will be transferred to the Shanghai Local Court today.

Lawsuit Over Millions of Family Fortune, Numerous Descendants, and Unequal Circumstances 156

Lawsuit Involving the Family of Minister to the United States, Shih Chao-chi

Nephews and Grandnephews Sue Over Property Division

The nephews, etc., of Minister to the United States, Shih Chao-chi, recently initiated a lawsuit in the First Special District Court over a dispute regarding the division of inheritance, which they failed to resolve peacefully. It is reported that Shih's uncle, Shih Shao-chin, had five sons: Tzu-ming, Tzu-ching, Tzu-hsuan, Tzu-ying, and Tzu-hsiang. All served as Tao-tais during the late Qing Dynasty. Tzu-hsiang then had five sons: Hsi-yuan, Tao-yuan, Pin-yuan, Hsin-yuan, and Chuan-yuan. Shih Chia-gu and Chia-hong, the current plaintiffs, are the children of Tao-yuan, who passed away the year before last, leaving behind his wife, Jiang Cai-zhen, who remains a widow and raises her orphaned sons. The defendants named in the lawsuit, Shih Lian-yuan, Bing-yuan, Jun-yuan, Zhen-yuan, Pin-yuan, Hsin-yuan, Jia-hua, Jia-zhen, etc., are either Tao-yuan's siblings, direct cousins, or nephews, all uncles and brothers of the two plaintiffs. According to their petition, plaintiff Jia-gu is only nine years old and suffers from a debilitating illness, making his treatment and care especially difficult. Plaintiff Jia-hong is only ten years old. Both depend on their mother for survival. Since the time of their great-grandfather Shao-chin, the family's assets have never been divided. Although estimated to be worth millions, the descendants are numerous and vary in age. Those who are older and influential possess vast wealth and live luxuriously, while those who are young and weak lack the resources for proper upbringing and education. For instance, defendant Zhen-yuan occupies a residence in the Dade Lane on Xinzha Road, defendant Jun-yuan occupies a residence in the Zhengxiu Lane on Kaifeng Road, defendants Pin-yuan and Hsin-yuan occupy residences in the Tangjia Lane, and defendants Jia-hua and Jia-zhen occupy residences in the Hengyuan Lane on Tianjin Road. These are all large buildings. There are also other movable and immovable properties that are difficult to ascertain at this time. The defendants are forcibly occupying the shared assets, taking whatever they want for their own enjoyment, while the plaintiffs are being deprived of their rightful share, leaving them unable to manage. In terms of human sentiment and legal principles, this is unfair. Therefore, they submit Shao-chin's family tree and request that the court order the defendants to hand over all of Shao-chin's inheritance for fair division according to the law. The day before yesterday afternoon, Judge Shen Hong presided over the hearing. Three of the defendants, Shih Bing-yuan, Lian-yuan, and Jun-yuan, hired lawyer Zhu Sifu to represent them in court. Both sides presented their points of contention. In addition, defendant Shih Zhen-yuan's wife, Ms. Wang, also appeared and expressed her views on how the Hengyuan Lane property, currently occupied by Zhen-yuan, should be divided. Judge Shen then stated that the case was very complicated and adjourned the hearing for further investigation and examination at a later date.

Ice Thawing Gradually, Fog Last Night

According to Datong News Agency, since the sudden cold snap that began on the 14th of this month, all ditches in the city have been covered with a thin layer of ice, and household water also freezes, thawing only after noon. By yesterday, the weather had warmed up again, and the wind direction shifted from northwest to northeast. Although still cool, it was no longer bone-chilling. Checking the calendar, today is the Great Cold solar term, marking the end of winter and the return of yang energy. Therefore, it is speculated that the winter will not be too cold, but spring chills should be guarded against. If, after the beginning of spring, there are continuous rains and snow, the agricultural harvest for this year will be a cause for great concern. Furthermore, starting around 7 PM last night, the city was again shrouded in fog, making visibility quite poor at a distance.

Labor Holiday Special Trains Started Running on Two Railways Yesterday 160

Departing from Shanghai at Noon, Returning from Zhenjiang Today

Stopping at Eight Stations Including Suzhou, Wuxi, and Changzhou

To facilitate Shanghai laborers returning to their hometowns for the winter holiday, the Railway Bureau has specially arranged third- and fourth-class special trains between Shanghai and Zhenjiang. All preparations have been completed by the Traffic Department, and the service began yesterday. The trains will stop at Suzhou, Wuxi, Changzhou, Benniu, Danyang, Xinfeng, Zhenjiang South Gate, and Zhenjiang stations. The details are as follows:

Special Train Organization 161

The special train will run once a day in each direction, consisting of two third-class cars, nine fourth-class cars, two baggage cars, and four boxcars, totaling seventeen cars. The cars originally assigned to trains 41, 42, 71, 72, 73, and 74 will also be organized in the same manner. The cars used for the special train may be adjusted as necessary. If there are too many passengers and not enough space, additional passenger and freight cars will be temporarily added to form an additional train. The boxcars will be lit with lights used for air raid drills. Long wooden benches with backs will be used as seats. Toilets will be temporarily installed in the corners of the cars, screened off with cloth curtains. For boarding and alighting, the lower part of one of the three window panels will be used, with steps added for convenience.

Departure Times 162

The service will run from January 20th to February 3rd, and again from February 9th to February 24th. The departure time for the outbound train is set for 9 PM every day from the Shanghai North Station, but it may be adjusted earlier or later depending on circumstances. The inbound train is scheduled to depart from Zhenjiang at 9:50 AM on the following day. It will stop at eight stations: Suzhou, Wuxi, Changzhou, Benniu, Danyang, Xinfeng, Zhenjiang South Gate, and Zhenjiang.

Ticketing Procedures 163

At the Shanghai North Station, the chief stationmaster will be responsible for managing the ticket sales. The Shanghai First and Second Business Offices will assist in selling same-day tickets. After the tickets are sold, the total number must be immediately communicated to the Shanghai Chief Stationmaster by telephone. If individual passengers have too many belongings and cannot purchase tickets themselves, the station will designate a location for storing items, and staff will be assigned to look after them and provide temporary numbered tags to the passengers for safekeeping, so that they can purchase tickets. To expedite the handling of passengers' free baggage, numbered paper tags will be used. Each piece of luggage will have a tag with a number, and a matching tag will be given to the passenger. Items can be retrieved by matching the numbers upon arrival.

Mr. Mi Qianliang's Purchase of Chinese Floral Carpets 166

Considerable Effort in the Process

Ultimately Succeeded Against the Clock

Shipped to the United States as Scheduled

The North China Daily News reported, "Success or failure depends on winning against time, which can be proven anywhere. In this case, Mr. Mi Qianliang was fortunate enough to win against time; otherwise, his months of hard work in China would have been in vain. Mr. Mi was commissioned to come to China to purchase floral carpets for the opening of the New York Exhibition on the 11th of this month. After arriving in Shanghai three months ago, he went to Beijing to have 170 different kinds of floral carpet samples woven, each measuring four feet by two feet. Once completed, they were packed into six large boxes (each five feet long and three and a half feet wide and high) and he took them on the Blue Express train heading south, intending to arrive in Shanghai on Friday morning and immediately board the President Taft mail steamer back to the United States. Unexpectedly, according to railway regulations, he could not carry them with him, causing Mr. Mi great disappointment, as if he shipped them on the next ship to the United States, they would likely not arrive in time for the exhibition. Therefore, Mr. Mi consulted with the Shanghai Moutai Company and requested assistance from the Shanghai Municipal Council Police Department, railway authorities, the mail steamer company, the manager of the Eastern Passenger Agency, the Nanjing government, and the Jianghai Customs. The only thing he could not negotiate was the tide, as the President Taft steamer needed tidal power and had to weigh anchor at 8 AM on Saturday morning, regardless of whether the carpets had arrived on board. Since Mr. Mi was restricted by railway regulations from carrying the carpets with him, he immediately set off for Shanghai to find another way to catch the steamer, leaving his representative on the train to negotiate with the railway authorities to have the boxes transported by express train the next day. The train was scheduled to arrive at the North Station at 7:40 AM on Saturday, leaving Mr. Mi and his assistants only twenty minutes to transport the boxes to the President Taft, which was anchored midstream in the Huangpu River four miles downstream from the Waterworks Company. Previously, Mr. Mi had telegraphed the relevant authorities to ask for their cooperation. On Friday, Moutai Company also contacted the police and other parties, and drove in a car from the North Station to the wharf for a trial run. The police agreed to provide special convenience for transporting the goods, and the driver of the car from the Waterworks Company also agreed to lend its wharf. However, for ease of loading and unloading, it was decided to use the new wharf built by the Shanghai Municipal Council on Qiwupu Road. The drive from the North Station to the wharf would take twelve minutes, but as loading and unloading would take some time, it was quite worrying. Fortunately, a motor vehicle from the police department would escort them, so there should be no mistakes. On Saturday morning, the train arrived three minutes earlier than scheduled, thanks to the enthusiastic assistance of the railway authorities. With the help of the police managing the North Station, the car was parked in a particularly convenient location on the platform. Therefore, six minutes after the train arrived, the six large boxes and Mr. Mi's luggage had been loaded onto the car, which then sped along the Concession Road, Henan Road, Bazi Road, Faelun Road, Suzhou Road, across the Broadway Bridge, and then along Broadway Road, Yangshupu Road, and into Qiwupu Road, reaching the wharf. The four-mile journey was completed in nine minutes, three minutes faster than the twelve minutes of the trial run on Friday. Within two minutes, the boxes had been moved from the car to the lighter. After another minute, the lighter had reached the President Taft. The lighter sounded its whistle to inform the crew that Mr. Mi and his luggage were arriving. The crew also knew about this and had made all the preparations, waiting only for Mr. Mi and his luggage to board before weighing anchor. At that time, only customs officers were standing on the pontoon bridge, briefly inspecting Mr. Mi's luggage. Then, with a whistle, the President Taft raised anchor and set sail at 8 o'clock. The ship is scheduled to arrive in San Francisco on February 5th, where the carpets will be exhibited. The next day, they will be exhibited in Los Angeles, and on the 11th, they will be displayed at the New York Exhibition. Therefore, Mr. Mi still has a lot of work to do after arriving in the United States."

Sent to Hospital for Treatment in Critical Condition
