Etiology, Treatment, and Prevention of Pyorrhea Alveolaris (2) 237

— Lin Jianxian

(2) Treatment of Type A Pyorrhea Alveolaris

—Surgical Treatment—

(1) Scrape off tartar. Tartar is the main cause of this disease and must be scraped off. Special instruments must be used when scraping to avoid injuring the gums, periodontal membrane, and teeth.

(2) Extreme caution must be exercised when performing surgery to prevent hard tartar from flying into the eyes of the doctor or the patient.

(3) Before scraping tartar, the patient's mouth must be rinsed several times with a disinfectant to wash away the dirt in the mouth (commonly using cinnamon water with 2% alcohol).

(4) The tartar scraping operation must be performed in order. First scrape the teeth of a certain part, so that the tartar is completely scraped off, and then scrape the teeth of other parts. Do not scrape randomly. It is best to place various instruments on a special tray soaked in a palatable disinfectant.

(5) The pocket of this disease is very shallow, and the tartar is easier to scrape off. The scraping time is limited to one hour. After scraping, use silicon whetstone, orange tree bark, pumice, floss, and brushes to scrub. The teeth of this disease are not shaking and do not need to be fitted with appliances.

—Drug Treatment—

(1) After the tartar is scraped off, a disinfectant must be used to wash away the tartar debris and pumice powder scraped around the teeth. Wipe the affected area dry with a cotton roll, and then apply a suitable astringent (such as a mixed solution of Zinc phenolsulphonatic, potasufodidi lodi, mentholis, etc.) to the gingival area and interdental space. Keep it for a few minutes, and then rinse with a disinfectant. This treatment should be performed each time until cured.

(2) Patients must also pay attention to oral hygiene at the same time. Wash and rub the teeth and gums every day, and rinse with a disinfectant frequently.

(3) In recent years, the use of 5% Dichloramin-T dissolved in chlorocosane injected into the pocket has been quite effective.

(4) Astringent mouthwashes must not be used, because long-term use can interfere with the fermentation effect of saliva. If it must be used, it is best to make it into toothpaste and use it to brush the teeth and gums.

(3) Treatment of Type B Pyorrhea Alveolaris

—Surgical Treatment—

(1) If there is hard tartar, it must be completely scraped off and rinsed clean.

(2) If hard tartar is not easy to scrape off, chloroglucin_sulphuric acid can be applied to the deep part of the pocket first to make the tartar disintegrate and disperse, and then scrape it off.

(3) If there is no tartar, the pocket must also be washed and scraped clean before drug treatment can be performed.

(4) Too many teeth should not be treated at a time. About one to four teeth are the limit.

(5) If there are teeth that cannot be treated, they must be removed to avoid infecting other teeth.

(6) If the upper and lower teeth are not properly occluded, causing excessive pressure on a certain part of the teeth during chewing, measures must be taken to correct the occlusion. Smoothly grind the protruding and overly high occlusal surface with a whetstone, so that the entire occlusion is even. However, when grinding, the shape and beauty of all the teeth must be taken into account, and too much should not be ground off to avoid injuring the pulp.

(7) For those teeth whose pockets are very deep and the vitality of the pulp is weak, or those who need to be fitted with metal to firmly implant other shaking teeth, or those whose sensation is too sensitive, it is advisable to remove the pulp.

(8) Sometimes, various surgical procedures and drug treatments are performed, but the results are not good, and there is no effect, and the pocket still exists. At this time, the pocket is mostly deeper than five millimeters. In fact, there is no way to prevent its infection. The outer wall of the gums that form the pocket must be surgically opened to the bottom of the pocket, or cut into a V shape. Scrape off and wash away the internal tartar and toxins. For severe cases, the gums must be completely cut open, and then the dead bone of the alveolar bone and the granulation tissue of the affected area must be removed to achieve the desired effect.

—Drug Treatment—

(1) The astringent treatment used for type B pyorrhea alveolaris is the same as that for type A, but the treatment time is longer, and continuous treatment takes about two or three weeks.

(2) If you encounter a stubborn and difficult-to-treat purulent cyst with constant pus flow, the pus sac must be corroded with 125% to 50% phenolsuPhric acid (other acidic drugs cannot be used).

(3) Emetine treatment. Many buccal amebas (Endameba buccalis) and various parasites are often found in pyorrhea alveolaris pockets. Emetine treatment can be used to eliminate microorganisms and prevent suppuration. The following two emetine treatments are effective:

For subcutaneous injection, 0.5 centigram of emetine hydrochloride is prepared as a solution and injected subcutaneously into a suitable part of the body. Once a day. After about three or four days, inject again every one or two days. Buccal amebas can be eliminated in about six days.

Oral tablets. Take Alcresta lpecac Tablets orally three times a day, two tablets each time. Take with lukewarm water one hour before meals. After about five days of taking, you can stop taking it for seven days, and then continue to take it for five days. This tablet must be taken when surgical treatment is performed or before treatment. During the period of oral administration, it is fine if mild diarrhea symptoms appear. If diarrhea increases, you can stop taking it for three or four days. Ipecac tablets are not only strong in eliminating microorganisms, but also can treat lax and easily bleeding gums and inflammatory symptoms caused by local irritation.

(4) Ouinine and Urea hydroobloride treatment. Applying this medicine to the affected area can not only eliminate buccal amebas and spirochetes, but also has an acidic corrosive effect. When using this medicine, first wash the pocket clean and dry it. Then, put a pill made of this mixture on a glass slide, add two or three drops of distilled water, mix it into a paste, and send it into the pocket. Seal it temporarily with Vaseline ointment. After about five minutes, wash away the medicine in the pocket with warm water and scrape it clean. After using this medicine, it is best to use a corrosive to eliminate granulation tissue in the affected area. You can use Copper Sulpbate and 8% Zinc Cbloride made into a thick paste. After washing and drying the pocket, insert the paste into the pocket and rub it lightly to allow the medicine to penetrate into the bottom of the pocket. Then use Vaseline or (Chloro_percha·) solution to temporarily seal the mouth of the pocket, and then apply iodine to all the gums. After three or four days, perform the same treatment again. It should be cured in about three to five times. If the pocket has not shrunk at this time, it will heal. Then it must be removed surgically.

(5) If all kinds of drug treatments are ineffective, then surgical removal can only be effective.

—Appliance Fitting Treatment—

In addition to surgical treatment and drug treatment, very shaking teeth must be firmly implanted by using appliance fitting method. The so-called appliance fitting method is nothing more than the following types, namely gold crowns, bridge teeth, gold inlays, gold veneers, and various metal retainers. It is a method of fixing shaking teeth with appliances.

A Brief Discussion on Pulmonary Tuberculosis (3) (10) (8) 238

— Hu Jiayan

(6) X-ray Diagnosis

In today's society, there is a very popular old saying that is often used to praise doctors, called: "Penetrating insight into the crux of the problem." This is of course an exaggeration, and even those who have experienced it feel the same way; but if it is used to express the value of X-rays in diagnosis, it is no more appropriate! The author dares to say that, apart from the pathological anatomy aspect, the recognition of the nature of this disease is undoubtedly second to none due to it. It is true that the physical examination methods mentioned above, such as auscultation and percussion, are indeed similar to it in recognizing the current symptoms. However, physical examination is only an indirect procedure, and whether the technical training is proficient is a major difference; to put it another way, even if this difficulty is completely avoided, the range that it can reach is also a certain distance. If the location of the lesion is too far from the lung surface, there is absolutely no way. It is not like X-ray examination, which only needs to be fluoroscoped, and everything about the size, density, and form of the lesion can be seen at a glance. Therefore, its application in this disease is that almost every patient should undergo this examination procedure; even people who are suspected of having this disease mostly use the results of this aspect as the final confirmation.

What principle is X-ray based on when applied to medical diagnosis? The speculation of ordinary people is that it is used to view the internal organs with a mirror, which is completely hearsay and meaningless. We must know that X-rays have great penetrating power, which is certainly no exception for the human body; in addition, it can make objects with fluorescent function, such as Barium_platinCyarun, emit fluorescence. If you place a Barium_platinCyarun plate (i.e., fluoroscopy plate) in front of an X-ray beam, you can see the bright green phosphorescence emitted. If the human body is placed in between, then because of the different properties of various objects, different shades of influence will appear; like blood and bones show dark shadows, and muscles show light shadows. The lungs are organs containing air tissue, so X-rays can pass through and show the lung field on the transparent plate. Therefore, we can also check the pathological tissue and the existence of foreign objects according to the density of the shadow.

Free Talk

Not a Grievance 239

— Xi He

The Japanese writer Ryunosuke Akutagawa wrote for many years, and then one day, as if he were mad, he wrote in a book: "Why do we engage in literature?"

This question may sound ridiculous at first, but it contains great wisdom, and it will give you endless and profound aftertaste. We work diligently every day, studying "literary" books at our desks, and writing down our own feelings, but we lack an opportunity to sincerely reflect on this activity. Once we hear someone else point it out, we suddenly realize as if waking from a dream that these are actually just the most superficial and ordinary principles, which few of us have ever uncovered. In this short life, perhaps some people will learn and decide on a turning point in their lives, while others will continue to read and write, and when their great opportunity arrives, they will be filled with regret, or perhaps they will die in a state of confusion.

Indeed, why do we engage in literature?

According to the French philosopher Voltaire, he wrote to express what he thought, but this answer is too mysterious. Arishima Takeo said that he wrote for four purposes: first, for loneliness; second, for love; third, for the desire to love; and fourth, for the desire to spur on his own life. This answer is more to the point, but besides writing, aren't there more ways to achieve his ideals? Writing morning and night, taking literature, which people take least seriously, as the foundation of one's entire life, and presumptuously trying to clarify the world with a three-inch writing brush—this idea is truly adorned with the colors of Don Quixote. It's hard to imagine that someone with Arishima's courage could be so ignorant in this respect.

Just look at history vertically and at various ethnic groups horizontally. Aren't countless intelligent and wise people learning literature and writing there? Their ideals are different, and of course their writing goals are also different. Take our country as an example. Some write to pass on their names, some write to advance their careers, some write to get稿费, some write to get love letters from women after publication, some write to boast about their hometown, some write to vent that "smoke-like sorrow," some write to praise each other, and ultimately, there are plenty of people who sing for losing money, as Ruskin said. Of course, there are also some who write seriously, wanting to use literature to shout out their ideals and pursue their longing for light, but besides "writing," what exactly do they accomplish?

Here, I am not denying the usefulness of literature. Literature is a means of organizing life and can have a significant impact on society. Turgenev's "A Sportsman's Sketches" promoting the emancipation of serfs is the best example of this, but my point is that a person who truly understands life does not engage in writing white words on black paper. He despises all trivial activities and uses his entire life to write the great book of "history." He may never pick up a pen in his life, but the achievements he makes in silence are enough to make these so-called "literary figures" sweat with shame!

Once we see such a rich and beautiful life, then we, the people who play with the magic of words, who use new skills to earn a living, who search for chapters and extract sentences, who spread out flowery language, and who emit smoke-like fantasies, are still shamelessly saying that we are the noblest people in the world, which can be said to be somewhat thick-skinned!

Listen to Bazarov's words in Turgenev's book:

—Russia needs me... no, obviously, it has no such need. Who is needed? Shoemakers, tailors, butchers... selling meat to people... butchers...

A literary person can be made or not made, someone has already said that before me, but my point is, if we only write some boring things, then it is better to be a shoemaker, a tailor, or a butcher. Even if we write, we must avoid being called a "literary person" by a certain group of people, which is not a very pleasant term.

A Record of Crossing the Ridge on a Snowy Night (Part 1) 240

— Xian He

It was already dark, but we still had to walk, which was truly disheartening. Even though we were walking quickly, the cold air of the deep mountains was sharply attacking from all directions, making us feel not a bit warmer, but even colder and unbearable. The wind was howling, its violent sound seeming to come from the dark sky, or as if it were rolling up from the cold valleys of the deep mountains. We only felt waves of阴寒, cutting into our bones like knives, but we couldn't discern the wind direction.

There was originally spring water in the mountain stream, flowing tirelessly day and night, passing through the trees and rocks. But at this time, it was also frozen, quietly and calmly, and we couldn't hear its low, gentle, murmuring song. Of course, the birds had also disappeared. The mountains floated in the heavy, turbid clouds,巍巍floating, as if the clouds couldn't bear their weight and were in danger of falling down at any moment. Thinking of that kind of mountain collapse, the earth-shattering sound, we all felt a chill, as if the ground was already shaking and spinning.

Crossing the ridge was especially frightening. The two upright mountain ridges were simply like two insurmountable, towering cliffs. It got deeper and deeper, narrower and narrower. You could only take one step at a time, never knowing if the place you stepped on next was safe ground or an abyss leading to your death. But discouragement was not an option. You could only move your feet firmly on the craggy rocks with a heart full of terror, not looking back or forward, because looking forward was clouds and fog, and looking back was also clouds and fog. Where exactly would it lead you, and who could know?

Most of the jungles along the ridge were old pine trees, dark and鬱鬰, and even in the deep, thick night fog, you could vaguely see the edges. The sky hung above the jungles, cold and lonely, seemingly clinging tightly to the treetops of the old pine trees. Apart from the difference in shade, there was no other boundary. I thought that on a clear night, the clear moonlight would shine on this蓊鬰, evergreen forest. When the mountain breeze blew, it would sound like surging waves everywhere, and the picturesque shadows of the pine branches would move everywhere, distinctly black and white. That kind of scene must be very poetic.

But surrounded by clouds and darkness, in this cold and freezing deep mountain, the pine wind was like the roaring of a violent tiger, the mournful cries of an ape, and the noisy howling of wolves. All poetic meaning had completely disappeared, leaving only terror,阴森, a kind of non-human, demon's bloody roar. Even when the cold wind blew a little lighter, they also lowered their voices a little, but it was still not as gentle and charming as when the sky was clear and the breeze was blowing. Nor was it majestic or cheerful. It echoed the cold wind, shouting and cheering, and that kind of violence would simply make one's teeth chill at the mere thought of it.

The road was very winding, sometimes to the left, sometimes to the right. Under our feet were all very sharp stones, and if we weren't wearing shoes, we would surely be cut until our skin was broken and bleeding. Sometimes it was so winding that it would simply lead you into some kind of mountain cave. Going in was not an option, and retreating was not an option. All around were rocks, dead grass, and dirty, frozen mud. If there were also stones pressing down on your head, it would be so dark that you could only grope around, and it would be a great blessing if you didn't break your head or scrape off your nose. Even if there was a stone crevice above your head, the light that shone in was very weak and blurry, and the wind also blew in, and the snow also drifted in, making it even colder than in complete darkness. Walking on steep slopes was especially difficult because the accumulated snow was very slippery, and a single tremor of the heart could lead to the danger of being smashed to pieces.

The thick fog gradually receded into苍白. Before, it was all pitch black, but now it was灰茫day. The wind was blowing very hard, and snowflakes began to fall. We held our heads in our hands, but the snowflakes still floated into our collars and drilled into our hearts. We were frozen stiff, and even shaking was unsuccessful, because our skin had all solidified and would not contract, and our bones were as hard as plaster models and would not bend. All over our bodies, we only felt a pain that pierced our lungs, seeming numb and seeming awake. A vague terror about ghosts and beasts rose like fog into our hearts, surging all the way up to our throats, suffocating our breath and hindering our thoughts. The whole world was spinning before our eyes and around us, and our feet seemed to be on top of a bottomless abyss that had just fallen in.

Skeptics in China 241

— Bai Lai

"The world is a big scam; life is a game; great poets, great writers... they are all big liars..." For many years, such teachings that emphasize skepticism to the extreme have been pouring into the blood of every young person like a torrent in literary production, theatrical performances, family admonitions, and mutual encouragement among friends. Thus, the younger generation of us is immersed in this atmosphere of skepticism, growing up, and rejoicing in our own "sophistication."

"Innocence" has become another name for "stupidity."

This terrifying phenomenon is deepening and expanding day by day, making me unable to help but think of what Arzibashev, the author of "Sanin," said through the mouth of a character in the book: "...If only my death could save humanity, I would be willing to die bearing the cross... but there is nothing in this world worth dying for..." (The general idea is like this) The archetype of skepticism, successfully emphasized in Arzibashev's writing, is widely present in China today.

Naturally, the mass production of skeptics has its roots in objective social conditions. Therefore, we can encounter many young people in the dance halls and bars of the city... using whiskey, women... to pass their every precious day, and they are successful as a philosophy of life to escape reality.

Now, if someone explains this phenomenon as "the decline of morality" or "the demise of ancient customs"... then we can only treat it as a dream that no one understands.

Parks and Me 242

— Di Zhou

I am a person who has no connection with parks. In the past, in other places, taking a morning walk on the long roads was one of my daily habits. Since my footsteps fell on the ground of this "international" commercial port, this habit has also disappeared because it could not be prolonged. But that doesn't mean I often go to parks as a result. On the contrary, except for special times, I only live in my house or rush about on the streets. Those who can connect with parks in their lives are only those who are comfortably well-off, or those above them.

The first park I came into contact with should be Hongkou Park. At that time, when I was very young, I couldn't help but feel a sense of sadness when I saw the团团yellow autumn leaves. I liked to stand alone, unfolding a broad vision, merging with the breath of nature little by little. I remember only going there three times in total, and the time seemed to be in the cold season. The mood of the last time was as if the heart and the scenery were one.

"Raging storm, come rolling in with the clouds! I expect, I look forward to,

I look forward to you bringing Byron's songs and the great power of the ancient Greek heroes!"

Singing such a song, my heart was hard to fill, as if a thousand kinds of emotions were expressed only in these two lines of song. In fact, the reason for forming such a mood at that time was not a deep understanding of society, which led to feeling something and thus worrying about the world and the country—but only being influenced by the literary content that was popular at that time, and giving rise to a dim vision of one's surroundings. —Even so, the indirect influence of the entire trend of society is undeniable.

About two years later, I went to Zhao Feng Park with a newly acquainted friend. It was a spring morning, and the warmth could already be felt in people's breath. The scenery in the park under the clear sky made me spread out my hands, as if falling into my mother's embrace, enjoying a moment of quiet rest. I thought, after heavy work, being able to come here and be comforted by nature for a while would restore fatigue! But thinking that those who could often come here were only gentlemen and ladies, and some drunken intellectuals, I felt empty and tired of the view of the tree trunks, the green buds, and the bright open space.

We started talking and immediately forgot about the surrounding scenery. Only the slightly sweet morning air constantly brewed new liquid of joy in my heart.

Shortly before this, I had entered the French Park. I was dragged there by someone, and I couldn't help but run there tastelesslessly. I didn't like that place. The "beautiful scenery" that was arranged gave people nothing but a sense of cliché and mediocrity. As for the Western children laughing in the cradle of paradise, their innocence, liveliness, and cuteness won the attention of general park visitors, but for me, they didn't arouse interest. What moved me slightly was the straight white path that connected Huanlong Road and led into the park, and the lush French parasol trees standing tall on both sides.

The most recent time I stepped into Zhao Feng Park was in the middle of spring this year. It had been three years since the previous time. The surface hadn't changed, just like the city it belonged to, but also like the city it belonged to, its inner essence had undergone a change. That was the triumphant faces of the Japanese. Men and women in Western-style clothes, smiling heartily, throwing simple volleyball-style balls. In addition, there were young people accompanying each other by the pool; middle-aged people, dragging canes, walking and talking in twos and threes. I thought: This phenomenon cannot be said to be unrelated to the expansion of Japanese power in this city. Obviously, even in the corner of leisure,木屐also showed her victorious posture with aggressive iron nails. I didn't stay long, quickly circled around, and left. This was for the same reason that I absolutely did not want to imprint my footprints on the French Park on the night of July 14th: I didn't like to witness other people's "威" and "glory."

Naturally, there are many birds and flowers in these parks, just as there are many ladies with施脂抹粉. But for me, they don't need to be seen with the eyes or heard with the ears, so there is no need to write about them with a pen. Recently, a friend came from the south and said that in City X, Jia, which was known for its parks throughout the country, only the rich姿 of nature was left, quietly enduring loneliness there. He said that the citizens of City X, for some reason, all didn't go there. After listening, I couldn't help but worry about the people in this "international" city. Perhaps one day, the parks here will also suddenly become desolate, and there will be朵朵株株"late summer roses" everywhere in the parks. (End)

The Human World (5) 244

— Li Huiying

Later, after my friend repeatedly proved and told her what a well-behaved person I was, never getting close to women, only wanting to broaden my horizons and see more things, that's why I brought them to see, and there was no other intention besides that. He also said some lies to compliment me, saying what a good person I was, how much knowledge I had, and how my mind was not bad, and explained that I had never used my position to find fault with others.

She put down her hand. This last lie seemed to touch her very much. A smile surfaced on her face, and she glanced at me, saying, "Then that's convenient for both of us, Director Li," and lay down on the炕surface and began to smoke. My friend closely followed and lay down opposite her.

This old friend of mine is not as honest as he used to be. He used to blush at the mention of women, but now, not only can he handle the affairs in front of him calmly, but he also teases women with vulgar and ugly words from time to time. The woman didn't avoid me, reaching out and touching him all over, and at the same time, he kept touching her.

"Is this probably the reason for the prosperity of private opium dens?"

I was thinking this when my friend tilted his head and asked me:

"How is it? This is a good place, right?"

The woman had already put an opium bubble on the opium pipe and handed it to my friend. He put it in his mouth and started smoking, and the opium pipe made a嗤啦嗤啦sound. The woman kept fiddling with the opium bubble with an opium needle.

"No, I can't stand it anymore! I have a headache! Do you have another room? Otherwise, I'll leave first."

Economic Supplement

A Glimpse into the State of Finances 245

— Zhang Yifan

(I) Causes: Internal and External

The financial panic in capitalist countries arises from two main causes. One is the intensification of their inherent contradictions; economic activity declines, resulting in a decrease in general tax revenues, leading to a shortfall in annual income. The other is the surge in their ambitions for external aggression, resulting in continuous and massive military expenditures, squandering the people's wealth on unproductive extravagances like guns, cannons and shipbuilding, thus inflating the state's budget. Simultaneously, there is a self-destructive effect of the internal system. The ruling classes in various countries, to safeguard the accumulation of their capital, use their political power to shift the burden of taxation onto the masses, and then, through means of using public funds for private gain, greatly increase expenditures on items such as relief funds, subsidies, and public works, in order to alleviate the general panic while accelerating the process of financial capital monopolization. Thus, on one hand, expenditures inflate; on the other hand, revenues sharply decrease, plunging the nation itself into impoverishment, reaching a tragic self-destructive state, and completing the process of financial panic.

However, in our country, the form of panic is naturally not entirely the same, but its severity far exceeds that of other nations. The origins of this state lie in other areas.

First: Our country is a semi-colonial nation, serving as a supplier of raw materials on one hand and absorbing excess commodities from capitalist countries worldwide on the other. When a surplus occurs in the global raw materials market, our international currency can no longer maintain its balance. Under a state of perennial trade deficits, the disintegration of the colonial economic structure is accelerated, and the national finances, parasitic upon this structure, are shaken from its foundation.

Second: During the process of military aggression by the great powers, they extorted huge reparations from us; and in the process of their economic aggression, they used investments and loans to shackle our throats with the iron chains of their financial capital. Under the heavy yoke of reparations and foreign debt, our national finances have been crushed.

Third: Our country has always been one with "wealth but no governance," and there are two reasons for this situation: one is the political disarray, which leads to long-term chaos in financial activities. The other is the poisoning effect of traditional thought. Chinese gentlemen have always looked down upon the study of financial management, with the saying "a gentleman does not speak of profit," and "rather have a thieving minister than a minister who hoards." Everyone has adopted this passive attitude, which has resulted in the unrestrained pursuit of private gain by "ministers who hoard." Consequently, even if there is governance, it is merely arbitrary extraction and arbitrary distribution. After accumulating such bad habits for so long, it is naturally more difficult to turn the situation around now.

Fourth: The rampant feudal forces have created political disunity, making it impossible to unify finances. The current situation may be said to have progressed considerably, but the remaining feudal forces have not been completely eliminated. Therefore, although there have been loud calls for reorganizing finances in recent years, these efforts are often hampered by various political constraints.

Fifth: Because the intellectual class looks down upon finance, there is a particular lack of specialists in financial management. At the same time, "auspicious" individuals all regard financial positions as a shortcut to wealth. Customs and tax officials all view their offices as lucrative positions, so there is rarely any integrity. Although the central government has repeatedly issued orders and decrees, there are still many who openly defy them in secret. For example, last year's exposed cases of corruption in land taxes were too numerous to count. Such as the joint embezzlement of tens of thousands of yuan of tax funds by the Songjiang County government; such as the more than ten land tax fraud cases in Shuyang, embezzling more than 100,000 yuan of national tax annually; such as the Suzhou collection director Mr. Zhu's embezzlement of more than 500,000 yuan of national taxes; and such as the joint contracting of registry clerks in Suining County to form corrupt groups, etc. These are only the publicly exposed cases; how many unexposed dark secrets are there? Therefore, with finances wasted and governance in disarray, it is no wonder that the financial panic is becoming more and more severe.

(II) Forms: Different Then and Now

In recent years, the central government has made every effort to reform finances and eliminate long-standing abuses, which is truly commendable. Within the past year, it has shown a particularly determined resolution to address the issue of tax system reform. Although there have been no significant achievements yet, it is enough to excite us common people. Because if the tax system can be reorganized and revitalized, then the most difficult problems in finance can be said to have been largely resolved. However, in reality, the difficulty of the problem lies outside of the system itself. The chaos and unfairness of the current tax system are the crystallization of the five major causes mentioned earlier.

Our country is a semi-colonial nation, subject to years of internal and external erosion and disguised destruction. This situation has long plunged the nation into thorough poverty and complete bankruptcy. In recent years, the surplus in the world raw materials market has led to the bankruptcy of our country's rural economy. The urban economy, due to the hollowness of its lower foundation, has embarked on a path of disintegration. The financial economy, which is nurtured by the entire social economy, has reached a dead end. So, in the past, there was "wealth but no governance," but now we are almost in a state of "no wealth for governance." "Wealth but no governance" is just a matter of people; solving personnel problems is relatively easy. But "no wealth for governance" is a factual problem: and factual problems have difficulties beyond human power. The saying goes, "a clever wife cannot cook rice without rice," which is the most fatal thing. The current emphasis on the slogan of reforming the tax system may be due to this. If reforming the tax system is carried out because of this reason, does this truly demonstrate the significance of reforming the tax system? Let us not delve into that for now, and instead, let us first examine the financial background of reforming the tax system.

(III) Crisis at This Stage

The countermeasures we hear about today for balancing the budget always involve increasing revenue and reducing expenditure. Does the currently advocated tax system reform represent the realization of this approach? Without going into that, we cannot help but doubt when we look at the current state of taxation in our country and its future.

Among our country's central tax revenues, customs duties are the primary source of funds. Since the Northeast customs duties were seized by the puppet state, their tax revenues still account for 52% of the total budget. In the previous year, when the Sino-Japanese tariff agreement expired, it was announced that the tariff rates on certain bulk imports would be slightly increased, so the amount of customs duties in the budget was further increased: its ratio to the total budget had increased to 53%. However, the actual revenue collected during the final accounting was still 5% less than the budget. However, in the past year, while the budget was being prepared, the budget amount of customs duties was increased. At the same time, the previous year's tariff agreement was abandoned, a new tariff agreement was re-issued, and the increased tariff rates were largely reduced to their previous state. This approach seems baffling at first glance, but those who understand the economic reason that two plus two is often less than three can also understand the depth of its intention. Reducing the tariff rates on bulk imports will inevitably increase the import volume of those goods, so it is hoped that the tax revenue from these goods will increase. As for whether this result will hit the domestic industry, that is another issue; but can this policy of robbing Peter to pay Paul be as successful as hoped? There is now evidence to prove it.

According to the national budget for the 23rd year, the projected revenue from customs duties was set at more than 380 million yuan, an increase of more than 30 million yuan compared to the projected amount of 350 million yuan in the 22nd year. However, according to the actual customs duties collected in the 23rd year (including the total revenue from import, export, transit, ship duties and surcharges, etc.) totaled 334.6 million yuan, a decrease of slightly less than 6 million yuan compared to the 339.5 million yuan in the 22nd year, and the amount of import duty reduction alone reached more than 3 million gold units, fully demonstrating the failure of the financial significance of last year's new import tariffs. The fiscal year for tariff accounting is different from the calendar year, but the recent sharp decline in foreign trade has revealed the decline in general purchasing power: therefore, even if this indirect tax method is used to increase tax revenue, it will ultimately be in vain due to the shrinking room for shifting the burden. Now the projected amount of customs duties has been increased in the budget, and at the same time, it is widely reported that the import tariff will be revised again. How to revise it we do not know at present, but no matter what, unless there is a way to safeguard domestic industries and improve the national economy, any severe fiscal and tariff policy will not work.

Let's look at salt tax, which is also one of the financial resources on which the central government places infinite hope. After the Northeast salt tax was seized by the puppet state, the projected salt tax revenue for the 21st year once fell by more than 20 million yuan. Now that the Northeast has not been recovered, the projected salt tax revenue in the budget has gradually increased. For example, the budget for the 23rd year has exceeded the record before the loss of the Northeast, creating an unprecedented record. For example, the salt tax budget for the 20th year before the September 18th Incident was more than 160 million yuan, but in the 23rd year, it has soared to more than 190 million yuan. This sharp increase in revenue is naturally the result of increasing the burden of salt consumption for the people in the country. Japan seized our Northeast and seized our financial resources, so the people in the country must bear this responsibility and compensate for this loss. In order to maintain national finances, this is the inevitable obligation of the people of an invaded country. Unfortunately, salt is an indispensable necessity for the daily lives of all people, and increasing salt tax revenue means increasing the burden of salt consumption for the people, which also means increasing the burden of people's lives. Regardless of whether the current means of rectifying salt affairs is only changing the weight of salt, without increasing the tax rate. However, replacing the 13.1-tael market scale with the 16.8-tael Sima scale has actually made the change in the tax rate quite significant. The recent surge in salt prices is a clear example. Now we have also heard about the plan to unify the national salt tax rate. The disparity in salt tax rates in various parts of our country makes it necessary to strengthen unification. But we are worried that the unification method is just to raise the low tax rate to the level of the high tax rate. According to the current highest tax rate, some places levy 14-15 yuan per dan: while the low tax rate areas are only 3-4 yuan, so if this method is adopted. Wouldn't that mean that the salt burden of the people in the low tax rate areas will suddenly increase by four or five times? The public sale of salt was originally intended to prevent the monopoly of market prices by unscrupulous merchants, and at the same time, it also allowed the state to increase financial resources in this monopoly. But its fundamental stand. Should take into account both social people's livelihood and financial tax revenue, that is undoubtedly, but what about now?

In terms of national taxes, we should also mention the consolidated tax, which is also an important financial resource for the central government. Although it has not been established for a long time, its position in the budget has been expanding infinitely. Its main collection target is national industry. In fiscal science, in order to universally distribute the tax burden, this is originally a considerable method. Therefore, we do not care about its impact on the social economy, and in terms of the purpose of finance itself, is there room for placing infinite hope, relying on the increase in this consolidated tax revenue to help the development of finance? We know that the position of the consolidated tax in the budget has increased from 9% in the 20th year of the Republic of China to 15% now. This means that its importance has increased by about one time compared to before. The projected revenue for the 23rd year has been set at more than 117 million yuan, so an average of 9 million yuan should be collected every month to achieve this goal. But the fact is that the actual collection performance in the first eight months of last year averaged only more than 8.6 million yuan per month, and the revenue in July was only more than 6.4 million yuan. Therefore, in order to make up for the shortfall in the budget, the tax rate will naturally be increased again, so the increase in the yarn and powder consolidated tax rate has now become the central government's inevitable goal, and it is only a matter of time before it is implemented. But we know that this shortfall in actual revenue means that its tax rate has already exceeded the taxpayer's limit. In other words, it is already above the national tax-paying ability. Now if we still want to increase its tax rate, wouldn't it be committing the fallacy of reversing cause and effect?

The central government is like this, what about the local governments? Everyone knows that the only financial source for maintaining local finances is land tax. Now it is under the slogan of rural revitalization, this is the only right remedy. But what is the actual effect? Let's discuss it later. Here, let's take a look at the farmers' existing burden to know what the direction should be taken when reorganizing the local tax system? According to the survey by the Central Agricultural Experiment Institute, the tax burden of farmers has increased in recent years. Their statistical results show that the burden of farmers in 687 counties in 22 provinces across the country has increased greatly compared to before. The average tax rate for paddy fields in each province was 2.07% of the land price in the 20th year, 2.37% in the 21st year, and further increased to 2.68% in the 23rd year. As for the tax rate for dry land, its increase rate is even greater, from 2.36% of the land price in the 20th year to 2.5% in the 21st year, and further increased to 2.8% in the 23rd year. According to Dr. Sun Yat-sen's teachings, it seems to be stipulated that only 1% of the land price should be collected. Are we now following this teaching and reducing taxes? Let's not ask for now. But in the midst of such an increase in the burden of farmers, can we solve the shortfall in local government revenue and expenditure? No, no, millions of facts tell us that the poverty of local finances is more severe than that of the central government. Taking the new budgets of the provinces in the 23rd year as an example, there is not a single province that is not in a state of huge deficit and emptiness. For example, Guangdong has a deficit of 50 million, Zhejiang has a deficit of 7 million, Anhui has a deficit of 5 million, Hebei has a deficit of 4 million, Gansu has a deficit of 3 million, Jiangsu has a deficit of 3 million, and Fujian, Hunan, Chahar and other provinces each have deficits of 2-3 million, and others are not known.

Under this huge deficit, what is their way to make it up? It is to issue public bonds. Localities that find the issuance of public bonds cumbersome simply implement loans. The names of the public bonds issued in various places and the reasons for the loans raised are all very grand and high-sounding. For example, Zhejiang, Fujian, and Guangxi have issued local public bonds, Hubei, Guangdong, and Xinjiang have issued financial public bonds or treasury bills, and Jiangsu, Henan, Zhejiang, Hunan, Hebei, Shandong, Fujian, etc. have raised new debts in the name of construction or water control and road construction. There are also silk cocoon loans in Zhejiang and Shandong, warehouse loans in Zhejiang and Jiangsu, and disaster relief public bonds in Hubei, Anhui, and Hunan. According to sporadic reports, the total amount of new local public bonds and new loans issued and issued by various provinces in the past year totaled more than 250 million yuan. The so-called public bonds and the so-called loans are the prelude to increasing taxes. Because their principal and interest payments are all borne by the masses, and they have also increased the burden of interest payments for the people, and have increased a "profit" for the banks and financial groups to obtain from the people.

(IV) What Strategy to Improve the Future

If we want to ask the question of "what is the best way to improve this situation?" then the frank answer is "earnestly reduce expenditure."

We should know that although the finances of various countries rely on taxes as their main support, none are as reliant as ours! For example, let's take a look at the examples of the financial budgets of various countries in 1934-1935; in the UK, out of 700 million pounds of revenue, tax revenue is estimated at more than 660 million pounds, accounting for 94%, which is considered the largest. In the United States, out of more than 4.4 billion US dollars, tax revenue accounts for more than 3.79 billion yuan, accounting for 84%, which can be listed as second. The third is Germany, in the revenue of 6.5 billion marks, taxes account for 5.2 billion, accounting for 89%. The next is France, the total revenue is 50 billion francs, and the tax revenue is 40 billion francs, accounting for 80%. As for Soviet Russia, it is simply very small. The total budget reaches more than 48.88 billion rubles, and tax revenue is only more than 33 billion, accounting for only 73%. Moreover, these taxes are all collected from the socialized economic sector, and the taxes directly collected from the people are only more than 2 billion rubles. But look at us! Then, in each year's total budget, taxes always account for more than 95% of the total amount. The French and Japanese cabinets are often overthrown by parliament for proposing tax increase proposals. Their national economies are hundreds of times better than ours, and they still express that tax policies are too harsh on the people, let alone us?

However, the facts are in front of us. In this situation of internal and external troubles, we must make plans to resist the strong and defend against violence. Therefore, we must have sufficient financial capital to engage in various constructions and necessary preparations. However, unless the social economy recovers a little, any empty talk is worthless. Under this dilemma, this contradictory situation, we should naturally implement a dual-track system, that is, on the one hand, we should stand on the standpoint of relieving the people's suffering, reorganize the tax system, increase tax revenue by eliminating long-standing abuses, and nurture the people by distributing the tax burden equally. If we can distribute the tax burden equally, reduce waste, and eliminate long-standing abuses, then although the tax burden of the people may not be reduced, at least they can get a sense of fairness and be sincerely convinced. This is also meaningful for finances, and can achieve the purpose of increasing revenue. But looking at the facts mentioned above, how much revenue can be increased, the hope is very limited! Therefore, the important thing is to cut spending and earnestly reduce expenditure! In other words, it is "live within your means." The author has repeatedly advocated this in this publication.

Reducing expenditure is also one of the slogans that our country's authorities are chanting today, but how it is actually done, we have to take a look at.

The two major floods in our country's financial expenditure are military expenditure and debt service. The expenditure of these two items constantly consumes the entire three major tax revenues of the central government. Therefore, our country's financial budget is actually the expenditure budget of military expenditure and debt service. Debt service is the root cause of the disease planted in peacetime; now we can only taste the bitter fruit, because the perennial revenue and expenditure have not been enough, and we have only borrowed and repaid debts, so the deeper we get into it, the inevitable result. In the past, we drank poison to quench our thirst, only caring about the present and not thinking about the future: now there is no way to think about it, and there is no way to reduce expenditure, so there is no need to talk about it.

As for military expenditure, in the past, it was for resisting Japan and suppressing bandits. Suppressing external aggression and pacifying internal unrest were carried out at the same time, and the expansion of military expenditure was originally an unavoidable necessity. Now the lost land has not been recovered, and the powerful enemy is still invading. However, the work of suppressing bandits is said to be coming to an end. But in order to make the suppression of bandits successful, President Chiang has long said that we should spend 30% on military affairs and 70% on politics. If we do not earnestly restore the bandit areas today, the future troubles will still be difficult to eliminate. In this way, today's administrative expenses will naturally have a considerable increase compared to before.

However, no matter what, the new budget for the 23rd year has not achieved the principle of "reducing expenditure," which is undeniable. We don't need to say anything else, just looking at the fact that financial expenses still account for more than 9% of the total expenditure, we can imagine it. If we remove debt service, military expenditure, current affairs expenses, and subsidies from the total expenditure, then financial and precautionary expenses account for more than 45% of the central government's various administrative expenses, which is unprecedented in any country in the world. According to the facts, the four northeastern provinces were taken away by others. Amen, we can slightly reduce the expenditure of financial expenses in these places. Recently, the abolition of likin and the merger and abolition of collection agencies such as stamp licenses can also reduce a lot of financial expenses. However, the financial expenses in the new budget have increased by a huge amount of more than 6.92 million yuan, an increase of more than 400,000 yuan compared to the 6.5 million yuan in the previous year. No wonder Mr. Ma Yinchu, chairman of the Finance Committee of the Legislative Yuan, wanted to complain at the meeting? However, Ma's struggle succumbed to the reason that the "Ministry of Finance must be difficult to comply with," and as a result, Ma's opinions were only used as a reference when preparing the next budget, and the original budget was passed as it was. Then, as citizens, we can only place our hopes on the future!

A Review of the Gold Standard Market 246

— He Boxiong

(1) Price Fluctuations

The intensity of the fluctuations in the Shanghai gold standard market price in the 23rd year of the Republic of China (1934) was truly an unprecedented record. Looking at the overall gold price for the year, the highest price reached 1,087 yuan, and the lowest price was only 665.5 yuan, a difference of 420.5 yuan. The magnitude of the rise and fall is evident from this. The greatest driving force was in fact the threat of the United States' silver policy. The following is a record of the general situation of Shanghai's gold standard price fluctuations over the past year:

December of the 22nd year of the Republic of China (1933): The Shanghai gold standard market situation. In the first ten days of the month, international news was extremely chaotic, causing the gold market to fluctuate from time to time; among them, the United States' gold purchasing policy and news of stabilizing exchange rates were the original driving force behind the gold market's waves. Entering the middle ten days of the month, the gold market suddenly experienced a surprising low point, falling through the major barriers of 680 to 700 yuan in one day. This was because news of the U.S. President's approval of the Silver Agreement and instructions to purchase silver at a price of 64.5 cents per short ounce were transmitted, causing the gold price to plummet.

January of the 23rd year of the Republic of China (1934): The gold market was extremely stable.

February: In the first ten days of the month, the gold price was also very mediocre. Entering the middle ten days of the month, the gold market was particularly depressed. This was partly because the end of the lunar year was approaching, and all parties were closing their accounts, and partly because of concerns about changing the new settlement price (see Section 3) and swap operations. (Note: Gold standard trading is divided into futures and spot transactions. The trading period includes swap and delivery periods. Swap is the period of hesitation given to traders each month in the middle of the month to buy or sell. The delivery period is the delivery period for gold standard transactions at the end of the month.) Entering the last ten days of the month, market sentiment was still uncertain, and transactions were still not active. Towards the end of the month, the gold price rose sharply due to the severe decline in the silver market.

March: From the perspective of the long-term trend for the entire month, there was a gradual advance. In the first ten days of the month, foreign news was divergent, and the market price was uncertain. The issue of raising the U.S. silver price and the talk of safe exchange rates were particularly sufficient to cause huge waves in the Shanghai gold standard market, and the gold market became increasingly strong. In addition, the rumors of international silver issues were sufficient to boost the prosperity of the gold market. By the end of the month, the gold market was almost entirely dominated by the U.S. silver issue due to complex international news, resulting in an increase of about 9.3 yuan compared to the end of the middle ten days of the month.

April: The gold standard market situation. From the beginning of the middle ten days to the last ten days of the month, news of a delay in the U.S. silver issue emerged, and the gold market showed its brilliance and rose rapidly. This was because the U.S. silver bill made no progress, and President Roosevelt expressed his rejection of silver legislation. News of the Japanese government's intention to purchase pure gold also arrived, and the gold price had an aura of invincibility. Looking at the overall gold price for the month, the highest gold price reached 1,027.7 yuan. Since the devaluation of the U.S. dollar and the change of settlement price, the Shanghai gold standard market has been extremely chaotic due to the complexity of international gold and silver economic issues.

May: The gold standard rose sharply last month, but it soared even higher this month, with the highest price being 1,087 yuan. In the last ten days of the month, news of the U.S. President's imposition of a 50% silver profit tax caused the gold market to retreat slightly, with the lowest price being 991.2 yuan. This month marked the discovery of new high and low records for the Shanghai gold price since the change in the settlement standard, with a difference of 79.1 yuan, which was also a new discovery for this year.

June: Market sentiment was extremely stable, and the rise and fall of the gold price was also extremely subtle. Towards the end of the month, the gold price began to fluctuate slightly due to the UK's refusal to pay overdue U.S. war debts and the complexity of the silver issue, but the trend was slightly weak.

July: Market sentiment was also extremely stable. Looking at the overall gold price for the month, the difference between the highest and lowest prices was only 22.9 yuan, making it the most stable month of the year.

August: In the first ten days of the month, the U.S. re-emphasized currency inflation, and the silver price rebounded, causing a sudden drop in the gold market. The UK and U.S. silver prices soared, and the U.S. government announced that it would nationalize silver and stop silver futures trading. As a result, the exchange market was unusually loose, and market sentiment was greatly disturbed, exacerbating the decline. It was rumored that the Chinese authorities would take measures to prevent foreign banks from shipping large amounts of silver for export, or impose a silver tax. Large dealers rushed to short sell, and the price suddenly soared to 65.5 yuan. It was later rumored that gold was flowing out of the United States and that exchange rates were trending lower, and the price returned to 60 yuan. Towards the end of the month, it was suddenly rumored that the United States was planning to inflate its currency again, and buyers were hesitant, causing the gold price to fall again. This shows the complexity of the gold price fluctuations this month.

September: The gold standard market situation. The complexity of domestic and international news caused extremely drastic changes. At the end of the first ten days of the month, the Ministry of Finance issued an order to ban gold standard and foreign exchange speculation (see Section 4 for details). At the end of the month, the rise in London gold prices was sufficient to affect the market price of the gold standard. In the first ten days of the month, the price rose first and then fell, without drastic changes. In the middle ten days of the month, the Ministry of Finance did not allow the gold standard to be settled based on foreign exchange, but changed to using the tariff gold converted from world gold bars as the gold standard settlement price, and the market situation was chaotic. In the last ten days of the month, the foreign silver market and the Shanghai foreign exchange market continued to grow, and international news was extremely complex, causing drastic changes in the market situation, and the decline became even more severe. The average price for the entire month was only 906 yuan, the lowest in nearly five or six months.

October: Domestic and international news was divergent, and the rise and fall of overseas silver prices were relatively large. In addition, after the Ministry of Finance implemented the additional silver export tax and balancing tax on the 15th, the gold standard market situation became extremely drastic. Although the UK and U.S. silver prices did not fall excessively, the Shanghai market was characterized by foreign merchants' operations, tight exchange rates, and panic among Chinese merchants. Although they rushed to close their positions, it was difficult to succeed. The gold price rose so sharply that the highest price reached 1,025 yuan.

November: After the gold price surge last month, the trend was relatively calm, but at the end of the middle ten days of the month and the beginning of the last ten days of the month, the difference between the high and low gold prices still varied by more than ten to twenty yuan per day. Initially, there was a large outflow of spot silver in Shanghai, leading to tight silver supply and higher interest rates on foreign exchange. Later, the Ministry of Finance ordered the customs to strictly suppress smuggling, and transportation to various ports in the country also required the approval of the authorities and the issuance of passports before shipment. There were also various rumors that were beneficial to the long side, so the gold price gradually advanced sharply, and reached as high as 1,022.5 yuan on the 24th. The following is a summary of the Shanghai gold market over the past year.

Last week (January 14th to 19th), the Chinese Merchants Securities Exchange market changed from hovering to weak, and then from weak to falling. The entire week was almost completely in a state of weakness. The fragility of sentiment and the weakness of market prices were due in part to the decline of various industries, and in part to the changes in the political situation. The supply and demand on the trading floor were also unfavorable to the long side due to the large short positions not being covered and the retail arbitrage transactions not being swapped. Moreover, with the imminent implementation of the transaction tax and the approaching Lunar New Year, customer groups were shrinking, transactions were not active, and market sentiment gradually declined. Therefore, although the foreign exchange rate was gradually reduced, and had dropped to the normal level of 1.3 points on Saturday, sentiment was not slightly excited. This was because the funds returned from the inland areas were not active, which was significantly different from previous years. The recent tense political situation made people even more afraid. There were not many days left in the year, and the delivery date was approaching. The future was not optimistic. Looking back at the past week, the market hovered and weakened on Monday and Tuesday, and transactions were very light. Although the foreign exchange rate was small, the money supply was still tight, and the transaction tax seemed inevitable. The floating longs were slowly released, and Numbers 47 and 48, etc. were sold off by a slightly smaller amount. On Wednesday, the hovering was the most severe, and the rise and fall was only about 0.1 point.
