Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talking Points

Wei Wenxiu Remarries Wang Kuixuan 251

— Helpless

Li Yuanhong's concubine, Wei Wenxiu, recently remarried Wang Kuixuan as his wife in Qingdao. Wei is 43 years old, while Wang is only in his thirties, which society finds laughable. In fact, in ordinary families, it is not strange for a concubine to remarry, let alone for a main wife to remarry, which is not uncommon at all. Wei Wenxiu, because she was Li Yuanhong's concubine, is now remarrying, and society finds it a topic of discussion, saying that Wei Wenxiu is ruining the reputation. And the people in Li's mansion must also consider it a great shame and humiliation, a matter that disgraces the family, which is not surprising.

In the history of the Republic of China, human beings are equal. Although Li Yuanhong was once the President, even if Mr. Li has not passed away now, the President is no different from ordinary people when he leaves office. Moreover, the current law does not allow concubines, so even if a concubine has unruly behavior, even if the original husband is still alive, there is no way to report it. Now that Mr. Li has passed away, Wei Wenxiu has no absolutely unbreakable relationship with Li's family. Therefore, Wei Wenxiu's remarriage to Wang Kuixuan is a very ordinary and extremely common thing.

As for the theory of Song Confucianism that "losing one's chastity is a major matter, starving to death is a minor matter," it is originally a moral issue, which cannot be judged by law, let alone interfered with by bystanders. "A concubine's heart is like ancient well water, and she vows not to cause waves." This kind of secluded, virtuous, and chaste virtue was rare to find in the ancients, and even less likely to be found in modern people. And what about asking a modern concubine for it? "When the sky is about to fall, dark clouds rise, and when a mother is about to remarry, she hardens her heart." Therefore, since Mr. Li has passed away, and his concubine wants to leave the hall and seek to go, she can only be allowed to seek to go, wanting to play a new tune on the lute. One can only let her play a new tune, it is only Wei's own personality issue, and it has absolutely nothing to do with Li's family style.

As for the reasons for women remarrying, there are only three points: (1) sexual impulse; (2) economic pressure; (3) being intolerable by the family. Wei Wenxiu has served Mr. Li for more than 20 years, so there is no need to worry about economic pressure. However, Wei is already 43 years old, and marrying a husband in his thirties, her sexual impulse may be unavoidable. Furthermore, judging from what she said in her letter, that she cannot be tolerated by her descendants, it can be generally seen that Wei is not tolerated by the family. In such a remarriage, both parties benefit. In Wei's case, why not do it? Even in Li's family, removing this thorn in their side, what is there to deeply blame?

Some people laugh and say that Wei is already 43 years old, while Wang is only in his thirties, which seems strange to sell a big man small. In fact, this is also not a strange thing. Looking at the women of today, their vanity is very developed. It is often the case that young girls marry old men in their fifties or sixties. Then, Wang Kuixuan's wife, Wei Wenxiu, is probably of the same mind as the women. If she is not tempted by money, then it is a "mystery of life." He must believe that Wei is the concubine of the President, and that marrying Wei is like clinging to the tail of a steed and advancing even more prominently. Or, he may think that the concubine of Mr. Li is, after all, different from an ordinary concubine, so regardless of her age, she has a value to marry.

Now, the marriage system is almost a formality, so divorce cases are increasing every day. And the identity of a concubine has not been confirmed by law, so why should we pay special attention to the remarriage of Li Yuanhong's concubine? This is truly what is meant by saying that even Confucius has a lewd heart. Therefore, I explain its meaning to tell those in the world who consider this matter to be an anomaly.

Page 20

Winter Plum 252

— Little Oriole

The winter plum blossoms in the cold weather. It is because of the cold that its fragrance, excellence, and charming demeanor are particularly evident.

Its color is strangely endearing, with a pink outer layer revealing a red core. It does not require the support of branches and leaves, appearing tender like a young girl's cheek, radiating a smile. Within that smile, infinite charm teases people's hearts. Ah, this plump maiden!

Is it some kind of fascinating temptation? I couldn't resist buying a small pot and placing it on a corner of my desk. The stark, cold wind blows in from the window, so cold that it spreads throughout my body. After closing the window, where does this burst of fragrance come from? Looking back, the winter plum on my desk smiles again.

December is a sensitive month for me, a season of remembrance!

It was when the winter plum first bloomed that Wen left, wanting to fulfill her own imagination. She left so resolutely, as if she had complete confidence in her decision. Friends tried their best to persuade her, hoping she would deeply reconsider, but these efforts could not sway her even slightly. She had firmly believed that her ideal was correct, and only by following this path could she attain happiness.

A month, a year—time slipped away quietly, without a trace. In this ruthless passage of time, news of Wen disappeared. No, she was faintly forgotten among the people. Even if there were news, it would only be some lingering impressions in recollections.

In reality, after a woman gets married, all news about her ceases to attract attention. On one occasion, through indirect friends, I learned that Wen had given birth, and it was a boy. Logically, in an era when the patriarchal system had not yet been eliminated, this was a cause for celebration. However, conjecture cannot become fact, and sometimes it may even contradict the truth.

The weather is cold again, and the winter plum is exuding its pure, elegant fragrance. I don't know why, but every time I reach this time of year, I think of the winter plum and inevitably think of Wen's demeanor, which possessed the same hue as the winter plum. Therefore, I cannot help but buy one or two pots and place them on my desk. This seems to have become a habit, but a great miracle occurred. I never expected, no matter what, to see Wen in the winter plum flower market. Perhaps she didn't want to be discovered by me? She hurriedly prepared to leave, but it was too late.

Her face was thinner, and a few shallow wrinkles had appeared at the corners of her eyes. The color of the winter plum was gone. Where was the charm of her maiden years?

From our conversation, I learned that she had divorced, that her child had died, and that the reason for their divorce was based on "fading beauty." In the end, her eyes became a little red. Naturally, she was very sad and in pain.

I had no way to comfort her, and I didn't know why my feelings at that moment were so complicated. Returning home, I looked at the winter plum on my desk. Its scattered petals had fallen onto the book and into the pot. Its color was still vibrant, but its life was so short!

From Inland Invasion to the City 253

Thoughts Inspired by a Lunar Eclipse 254

— Ge Bai

Reading alone under the lamp, the sound of gongs, drums, and firecrackers suddenly rang out. In this silent winter night, it sounded like a bombing attack during wartime. I couldn't help but throw my book down and jump up. But I immediately heard the cheers and curses of children. When the news of the lunar eclipse that I had read in the newspaper surfaced in my mind, I chuckled at my own panicked behavior.

When I was a child, I also participated in this unique ceremony of our ancient country. Half of it was due to poor education. The teacher in the private school told us that this was the wild moon eating the domestic moon, and we should beat gongs and drums to drive the wild moon away. But we questioned the teacher with "otherwise" and the like, and the teacher had no answer. In fact, the private school system only allowed the teacher to question the students, and the students had no room to speak. Are these many children not influenced by poor education? So I thought that our educational attitude was too lacking in seriousness. Ten years of study under the window were for going to court to become an official, and studying abroad was also for becoming an official. Striving to study while being obsessed with the dream of being an official has now led to not even having a place to eat. Thinking about it, even forcing a laugh is too much. This is a digression.

However, many highly educated Chinese people who clearly know that it is not the wild moon eating the domestic moon also sacrificed their sleeping time to participate in this grand event. What do you have to say about that?

A few years ago, rumors spread that the night would not get bright, and everyone hoarded grass and stored grain as if it were New Year's, and felt unusually panicked about this dark period, as if the world was going to turn into a terrible place. However, from the rumors to today, the sun rises in the east at the scheduled time every day, and these people who pursue light are instead indulging in darkness. In the world of neon lights, the moon already has no place. Even if the wild moon eats the domestic moon, what loss do they have?

From this I thought of a story: Someone stood by the roadside looking up at the sky. Someone else saw it and was curious, so they also stood and watched. Then someone C, someone D... When A became aware, he was already surrounded by a crowd. Someone asked A why, and A said: "The bird I raised escaped from its cage and landed on the eaves of the house across the street."

The Chinese people's "blindly following the crowd" and "busyness with nothing" are the most outstanding skills. The less it concerns themselves, the more willing they are to put in effort, otherwise they feel uneasy. However, when it comes to truly helping others, they stand by and watch. Being called a "strange nation" is not without reason.

If the lunar eclipse at night is the wild moon eating the domestic moon, will everyone beating gongs and drums be of any help to the moon itself? Knowing that the lunar eclipse is a natural phenomenon in the sky, but also blindly making a fuss, what is the reason for this?

Returning to Tangshan 255

— Jing Yun

As soon as it dawned, two buckets of porridge water with hardly any rice grains were placed in front of Chen Afa. They ate it hastily, and Chen Afa and dozens of young, strong, new, and old "fan ke" (overseas Chinese laborers) came from "Bo Li Lang" field. "Bo Li Lang" means police station, that is, ordinary people call the police station "Bo Li Lang". Several "Bo Li Lang" (Police) in yellow uniforms walked on the shining asphalt road like escorts of prisoners.

Although it was in the morning, the tropical sun was baking hotly on their heads and backs, making them feel a little uncomfortable. Sweat the size of soybeans oozed from their foreheads and flowed straight down their backs, soaking their white twill cloth coats. However, they could not get the freedom to rest, and had to follow several "Bo Li" aimlessly along this smooth, slender asphalt road.

"Where are we going after all?"

"Are we being sent to 'Bei Lan' to build the railway?" ("Bei Lan" is located in the Gulf of Siam, the first place that Chinese ships pass through when entering Siam.)

"Or are we being sent to Meng Lak to repair the Royal Park?"

Everyone's heart hid this question, and Chen Afa was no exception, feeling as anxious as an ant on a hot pot! However, no one wanted to open their mouths to say it, silently, limping, dragging their heavy, sluggish steps.

Behind them followed a group of idle wild children watching the excitement, and they were increasing, jumping, shouting, and laughing and screaming.

Passing through each street, the shop assistants on both sides of the shops stopped their work and ran to the front of the shops to watch the excitement, staring blankly with their heads raised like watching a god's procession in the countryside during the first month of the year, and slowly discussing together—

(The general people of Nanyang call the motherland "Tangshan".)

"Probably not, there hasn't been any case recently, has there?"

"Maybe these people can't pay the 'poll tax' this year?" It is said that those who can't pay the 'poll tax' this year will be sent back to 'Tangshan' without mercy once they are found out…"

These words sounded very disapproving to the old "fan ke" Chen Afa's ears at this time. He thought that he had spent more than twenty long years in Siam, and he was confident that he could abide by his duties in his daily work, and dare not act recklessly, but diligently be a docile person. Siam was simply his second hometown! Although business in Siam had not been good in the past few years, and he could not find work everywhere, causing a panic of unemployment, he could not pay the "poll tax" to the royal family on time every year. However, the royal family's magnanimity was great, as long as those who could not pay taxes did a week of voluntary work for the royal family, they could receive a "poll tax" receipt for nothing. Chen Afa had received his "poll tax" receipt in this way for the past two years. Therefore, Chen Afa absolutely dared not believe in his heart the saying "those who cannot pay the 'poll tax' will be sent back to 'Tangshan' without mercy once they are found out."

The road became flatter and wider, which made Chen Afa feel a little different from previous years. Although he was very sure that he would not be sent back to "Tangshan," he was still a little anxious in his heart!

…" Someone in their team sighed in a low voice.

Suddenly, Chen Afa raised his head. The towering Customs House, solemn and stately, was already lying across the front. In the Menam River, the huge "Xia Long Du" steamer, as large as a small mountain, which opened back to "Tangshan," the huge black smokestack, was quietly spitting out black gas in clusters. Under the violent oppression of several "Bo Li," they were driven onto the ship like pigs. Then, Chen Afa's dream was shattered. He looked at the tropical-flavored buildings on the shore, the green grass, and the happy and relaxed pedestrians. He couldn't help but think of his expectations when he left his hometown on a "red-headed sailboat" to Siam, and his wife and son in "Tangshan" still looking forward to him sending money to support them, and this time he was being forced to return to "Tangshan" in a state of destitution. His chest felt as painful as if a poisoned arrow had pierced it, and tears flowed torrentially from his eyes.

Lane Elementary School 256

— Shi Weizhi

Reading advertisements is said to be more interesting than reading news sometimes. For example, in the classified advertisements in this city, you often have the opportunity to know the value of a dog and a person, and in other aspects, you can increase a lot of knowledge that you won't get from reading news! If there are any advertising wars, the situation will be even more lively and spectacular. Otherwise, as long as you are willing to be patient and flip through it, there is a lot of good material that can be selected into a collection of humorous articles.

Here's another example, for example, today's newspaper has an announcement about XX Elementary School changing bosses. The announcement is "declaring on behalf of" by a lawyer. This wonderful article from the village is buried...

"According to XXX Lai, XXX Elementary School Principal XXX has transferred the school to XX due to lack of time to manage it. All previous debts and entanglements of the school are the responsibility of Mr. X. In addition to drawing up a document, please publish it in the newspaper, etc. Declare on behalf of it as above, and all parents can go to XX Road to register for school affairs."

It's not easy to eat these days. What you hear and see is a sound of store closures and layoffs. Therefore, those who know a few words move their minds and gather a few like-minded comrades, rent a Shikumen (stone-framed gate) building, and open a Confucius-says shop (also known as Lane Elementary School) to make a living. Although this result may not lead to a life of abundance and honor for their ancestors, to put it nicely, "plain clothes are warm, and vegetable roots are fragrant" can be coped with.

As a result, a group of unemployed people feel that although there is no golden house here, it is still a place to eat. So you come, I come, and now it has become a situation where "there are schools in every lane, and no lane without a school" (lane means lane).

With more colleagues, naturally there will be some competition. The best way to compete is to win over celebrities to be school directors, and hang up the signs of first-class stars like theaters. In that case, why worry about not declaring "business is booming all over the world, and wealth is flourishing in all directions" and being full of customers?

Seeing that this strategy was very popular, they exhausted their efforts to save every penny to hang up the star signs. As a result, the stars still had to hang up the no-war signs and announce in the newspaper that they resigned from the school. (Not long ago...)

Page 21

Let's put that aside for now. If you have too many ideas, the paper tiger will be torn down, and some are because they don't have enough connections, so they can't find a star to hire from heaven and earth, so they have to sit on their cold benches in frustration.

Although many shops can form a market, we have an old saying that goes, "It's not a loss to run to three shops," and with more Confucius-says shops, customers will naturally have to choose those with "good quality and low price," so it is inevitable that several shops will have to post red paper signs to attract customers.

Therefore, it is useless to blame him with words such as insulting the purity and dignity of education. At the beginning of starting a business, who doesn't hope to achieve cheap and good quality? Who doesn't want to fulfill some of the obligations that citizens should fulfill? Besides making a living for themselves.

In desperation, they naturally have to "let others laugh and scold, I will do it myself." To talk about propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame, to talk about reputation and morality, you must first have enough to eat.

If some people still think that this kind of "commercialization of education" is still a bit "that," then let's just forget about this kind of high-sounding words. You see, the so-called prestigious universities and colleges are not bragging about the school's facilities to "attract customers."

It should be known that the so-called "lane elementary school" of Confucius-says shops is just a clever way for unemployed intellectuals who have no choice.

Yao Xiaoan Wang Pingqiu Qilin Leopard

China and the West (1040) 11:00 PM to 12:00 AM

Opening Chapter "Spring Night Song"

Chrysanthemum flowers bloom all over, whiter than cotton. The affairs of spring are coming to an end, and the song of farewell is passed on. The fallen flowers are still not swept away by the servants. It is the sound of despair. Poets and lyricists are not interested. The old oriole cries, but no one sees it. Fortunately, the spring is still there before the dawn bell. First, tell the banquet of parting before seeing off the spring light. Jade is on the curtain. The spring bamboo shoots are open, and the color and taste are fresh. Singing and clapper boards play on the table. Writing poems is divided into rhymes and quick questions. Suddenly, the east wind comes and bids me farewell. The south wind is gentle and continuous. There is another Du Mu who is sad about spring. He quickly whips the skinny West Lake in Yangzhou. There is also the poetic meaning of Lu You that spring returns. A boat of smoke and waves is exhausted. There is also the brocade screen person who sees the spring light as cheap. The sound of the oriole is round and slippery. Sad for the fallen flowers. Send off the flower fairy. The night wind is too crazy. I knew that the spring color was already gone and there was nowhere to appreciate it. Regret planting azaleas in youth. I knew that spring would return and still I would labor to send it. Jin Ling should have protected Chang Juan earlier. Now, the deep love of fragrant grass is sad and thin. Bury the smoke of the Green Jade South City in the east wind. Leave a section of Wushan cloud. The sound of spring will still be waited for next year. Wait until next year when spring comes early. When the apricot blossoms are red again (not in vain) Du Fu met Li Guinian back then.

Therefore, in these few days, the problem of this bridge has made the general villagers uneasy.

Shen Bao This City Supplement Movie Special Issue

"Young and Inexperienced, Good Fortune Turns into Bad Luck" Conchitsa Montenegro's Regret 261

— Xue Mei

Luck is not necessarily a good thing; it depends on how you use it. If you use it well, you can become famous overnight. However, if you don't use it well, you can miss opportunities and regret it. For example, Conchitsa Montenegro's experience can serve as a lesson for other lucky people. She has now realized her past mistakes and is trying to remedy them, but it is already a great effort. However, her ability to realize this early is still a sign of intelligence.

After her repentance, she said, "My good fortune is my bad fortune. I should be punished by Hollywood!" Why did she say such a thing? Let's talk a little about her past.

In short, she became famous too early and too quickly. Her luck was too good. She was young and inexperienced and didn't know how to use it, so she gained and lost her good fortune. Now that she is twenty-one years old, her mind has matured with her body, and she realizes her past mistakes and wants to regroup and start over. She has some talent, a talent for singing and dancing, so she can still stand her ground in Hollywood and climb back up step by step. She is currently playing a very important role at Fox. However, she might have already become a big star if she hadn't been so confused before.

Conchitsa Montenegro was a singing and dancing star brought to the United States from Paris by MGM three years ago. At that time, she had indeed reached the status of a star, and her future seemed very secure. However, that future did not materialize as expected. Step by step, her work gradually decreased, and her contracts were canceled and not renewed. Recently, in addition to performing dance skills everywhere, she has only filmed a few short films in foreign languages.

Conchitsa is a spoiled child with a temper, a young lady's temper, and cannot tolerate any grievance. She was born in San Sebastian, a famous summer resort in Spain. Her father was a high-ranking military officer, and her family was very wealthy. She has an older sister, and they both studied at a convent from a young age. Once, the convent held a charity singing and dancing performance for the poor children of the area, and that was the turning point in Conchitsa's life. Conchitsa and her sister danced. After they finished dancing, the teachers, students, and family members praised them, making little Conchitsa so happy that she became arrogant.

She told her mother that she wanted to go to Paris to specialize in dancing. Of course, her parents never refused this little girl's wishes, so they sent her to a very famous singing and dancing school in Paris. Conchitsa was a child with innate talent and extremely beautiful posture. So, at the age of thirteen or fourteen, she had already gained a good reputation in Paris. Later, she continued to perform on stage in major cities such as Berlin, London, and Madrid, further captivating audiences. By the age of fifteen, she was famous throughout Europe and welcomed everywhere. At this time, an MGM investigator signed a contract with her, inviting her to the United States to make movies. So she and her sister went to Hollywood together.

MGM had great expectations. Conchitsa also had great expectations. When she arrived in Hollywood, she rented a luxurious mansion in the most expensive area, bought a large car, and hired a chauffeur in uniform, making a great splash and becoming very popular for a while. But Conchitsa now says with regret, "I didn't have any mental preparation when I received so much glory at that time. Because of my arrogance and rudeness, I inevitably had conflicts with others and ran into obstacles everywhere. Sometimes the company asked me to change my hairstyle, and I felt that it was an insult. Sometimes I wanted to perform in a certain way, and the director asked me to perform in another way, and I felt like I had become someone's slave. I refused to listen to advice. Because I had only heard praise and compliments before, I had never been criticized by others. So every time I encountered obstacles, I argued and threw tantrums. Sometimes I even cried because I couldn't do what I wanted freely.

As a result, the MGM authorities became tired of it, the contract was canceled, and her status suddenly declined. She soon realized that if she wanted to gain a foothold in Hollywood, she had to change her temper, be harmonious, and cooperate with others. She was determined to exist in Hollywood. Although her sister had already returned to Spain, she couldn't bear to give up the taste of the glory she had once enjoyed. Her realization was: "Becoming famous too early and too quickly is a bad thing. Anyone who becomes famous too early and too quickly should swallow their pride first, otherwise, they will run into big trouble!"

Believe It or Not, Strange Things in Hollywood 262

— Fu

Li Que Dielikes saw a calf injured among a herd of stampeding cattle. He rescued it and bandaged its wound. In the evening, after filming the movie, he took the calf home, slept with it in the same bed, and slept for one night.

Frank Lee Trinkin always carries a tube of anti-virus ointment in his pocket. Before and after kissing, he uses it on his lips, no matter who the female star is.

Director Alvin Cowper now lives in the house that the mysterious girl Greta Garbo used to live in. But recently, he raised the fence by two feet. He said Garbo was not mysterious enough.

Director E.H. Griffith has been using a corn cob pipe for twenty years. But when the British novelist Hugh Walpole arrived in Hollywood, he used sixty-five pipes in rotation every day. It took four days to complete one cycle.

That is a true and reliable fact. The famous Hollywood dance director, Leroy Prinz, does not dance a single step himself.

Musician Vincent Roberts has a very rich collection of star signatures. Recently, someone was willing to pay 100,000 gold yuan for it, but he refused to part with it.

Charlie de Waal said that his entry into the film industry should be attributed to a poker game. He was originally a newspaper reporter, but he was fired by his employer because of a poker game.

Lionel Barrymore spends a full 120 minutes every morning applying makeup in the production of "The Mark of the Vampire."

A signed photograph of the famous German aviator Baron von Richthofen is now rented out by the owner for ten yuan a day.

— Yunmen

Douglas Fairbanks, who has been absent for a long time and is now divorced from Mary Pickford, his martial arts romantic style has always been loved by fans at sea. Mr. Fairbanks, in order to be careful in his later years, is unwilling to repeat his past success. Therefore, his works are impossible to see. Fortunately, the British London Film Company repeatedly persuaded him, and Mr. Fairbanks agreed to star in "The Private Life of Don Juan." Currently, the film has arrived in China and is being inspected in Nanjing. It will be released after "Lake Country Carnival." Don Juan, the great lover of the nineteenth century, his secret history and romantic traces, performed by Mr. Fairbanks on the screen, should be immortal.

Laurel and Hardy's slapstick feature films are indeed very precious. Since they became famous, there have only been two feature films. The ones that have been publicly screened in this city are "Sons of the Desert" and "Twice Two." But now the third work "Babes in Toyland" will be performed at the end of the year. Then, in the sound of firecrackers, the audience should prepare to laugh heartily.

Slapstick superstar Eddie Cantor only has one work a year. This year's work is "Kid Millions," which is produced by American Goldwyn and presented by United Artists. It will also be publicly screened at the Grand Shanghai Theater on New Year's Day. During the New Year, it is essential to receive this timely masterpiece.

The Enthusiastic Registration of Actors at the Central Film Studio 264

Since the Nanjing Central Film Studio began to recruit male and female actors, the registration has been very enthusiastic. It is understood that the studio is a state-run film production studio, and its management methods and film production plans will follow the methods of state-run film production agencies in the Soviet Union and Italy. Actors, if selected, have a very promising future. Therefore, young male and female students who are fascinated by movies are flocking to register. However, many people are not clear about the registration procedures, often making futile trips. According to investigations, applicants must have a front and side half-length photo, and a full-body photo, a total of three photos, and must measure their height and weight before filling out the registration form. The registration location is at No. 27 Tong'an Lane, Shilu, Sanma Road, International News Photography Agency.

(1)

In this year of the rise of sound films, people who can speak standard Mandarin will naturally have many, many advantages.

The Suzhou Film Studio is a small company that started with a few thousand dollars. Its debut work "Children's Light" has been completely filmed. Movie Novel

ForsaKing all Others (10) 266

— Suyin

Mary has decided to marry Dylan. They have chosen another good day. Everything is being arranged as before. Life is like a dream. Tomorrow, Mary will be Mrs. Dylan Duda again. But now she feels a little sorry for Geoffrey. She watched Geoffrey sitting across from her in her study. She said softly, "Are you angry with me? Is it because I'm going to marry Dylan that you want to go to Yemen?" Geoffrey lowered his head! Looking at his cigarette, he said, "I really don't have any reason to stay here anymore, so I'm going back to Spain, but I sincerely want you to be happy together." Mary said, "But, Geoffrey, is it... that day when you and Paula came to find us, was I deliberately too stupid..." Geoffrey said angrily, "You're not stupid, I'm too stupid. I'm suffering the consequences of my own actions, what else can I say?" Mary said, "What does that mean?" Geoffrey hesitated for a moment, then said, "For twenty years, you have been in love with Dylan, and I have been in love with you. I won't compete with others, I'm quietly waiting for you to leave him automatically, and then I'll tell you..." As he said, he raised his head and looked at Mary's face, but Mary's eyes were already filled with tears. She choked and said, "Oh, Geoffrey, you have to believe me. I didn't know anything." Geoffrey said, "Of course, you wouldn't know. But now, I can only wish you a happy future." Mary said, "Then you can rest assured. I will definitely be happy when I marry Dylan. He is a careful and considerate person. He even remembered to send a lot of popcorn when I was onstage that day."

At this time. Herbert walked in and said, "Geoffrey, it's time. The ship is about to leave." Geoffrey stood up. Mary also stood up and kissed him briefly. Geoffrey walked out without looking back. Herbert deliberately walked behind, and after Geoffrey walked out, he said to Mary, "This is what you should know, the popcorn was sent by Geoffrey, not by Dylan." As he spoke, he also left.

They all left. Mary stood alone in the middle of the room, her hands clenched into fists. Popcorn, it turned out to be sent by him. Geoffrey, that thoughtful, serious Geoffrey. She remembered the things from her childhood, Geoffrey treated her so considerately and tenderly, she felt a pang of sadness. She only knew then that the person she loved was Geoffrey, only Geoffrey. So she ran into the garden, found Dylan, and asked him breathlessly, "What would you do if I, like you, left someone in the chapel?" Dylan initially didn't know she was serious, he laughed and said, "Who gave you the idea to ask me this kind of question? Eleanor?" But Mary said, "Dylan... I'm talking to you seriously!" Dylan said, "I'm also talking seriously. Let's do it the same way tomorrow. I'll go to the chapel early in the morning. You come late at night. When almost everyone..." Mary shouted, "This is not the time to joke. I'm just asking you, what would you do?" Dylan saw that the situation was not right. This was asking him to think. How should he answer? He couldn't answer for a moment, and only said, "How do I tell my friends?" Mary heard this and couldn't help but shout, "What?" She burst into tears and laughter at the same time. Dylan couldn't help it and shouted loudly, "Mary, what's wrong with you? You're humiliating me! You can't treat me like that! I can't take it!" Mary cried and said, "Oh, you know you can't take it! You quickly think of a way to take it! Go chop down the forest... I got infinite benefits. You can learn to swim and ride a horse. Otherwise, cry until you fall asleep. You think about it yourself! I'm not doing it!"

She covered her mouth and ran wildly outward. Dylan chased and shouted behind her, but she didn't hear him. She ran straight to the pier and found Geoffrey. Geoffrey asked her with a straight face and without a smile, "What are you doing here?" Mary said, "Nothing... but I heard that Spain is the most beautiful in the spring." Geoffrey said, "That's right." Mary turned around, grabbed Geoffrey's sleeve, and asked him with a look of sincerity and fear, "Will they let a fool like me land?" How Geoffrey answered her, you guess for yourself! (The End)

费氏书于一九○○年单独越途帕米尔高原又三年被推为筹人所组织西藏探险队之领导者深入藏之东北部着有东北西藏一书包括极有价值之池图四册及关于励权物权族山川地心磁力之纪载若干册按研究中国地心磁力学者素称美俄科学家为最惟范围皆不及藏境自有费氏之记载关于我国磁力之学始有完全国表可禧其价值可知氏现正忙于计划对于我国内地磁力拟更作详之采察云

(6) A Newly Discovered Fire Well in Shanghai 270

— (Photo by Wang Kai)

In 1920, a well was opened in the Taizhou Guild Hall on Xinjiao Road, Xujiawan, Shanghai. By 1926, the well suddenly dried up and was filled in. Recently, flames suddenly erupted from the water pipe at the wellhead, reaching as high as a person. The flames burned continuously. The guild hall then built a short brick wall next to it and set up utensils on top to boil water and cook food. According to experts, this is because there is a large amount of extremely flammable garbage buried in the ground, which has produced a kind of marsh gas containing methane over time.

(7) Ms. He Peixian, Master of Laws 271

— (Photo by Huang Renyi)

Ms. He is originally from Jiangxi and studied at the University of Paris in France, where she obtained a Master of Laws degree. This is a photo of Ms. He arriving in Shanghai a few days ago after completing her studies and returning to China.
